PENAL CODE

Consolidated version dated July 5, 2018




- 2 - PPRREEFFAACCEE
On the initiative of the association for the dissemination of legal information
and judicial, and thanks to the synergy of efforts of a number of skills
judicial and administrative skills in collective work, between the years
2004 to 2009, consolidated versions of the penal code were published as
that it has been modified and completed, following the compilation of the whole
modifications and additions which were introduced by the legislator in
with a view to obtaining a consolidated and reliable legal text1.
In addition to the said initiative, the new version – subject of this
preface - includes the latest modifications made to the penal code
the object until June 4, 2015.These are the following modifications:
- Law No. 103-13 relating to the fight against violence against
women promulgated by Dahir No. 1 -18-19 of 5 Joumada II 1439 (22
February 2018);Official Bulletin No. 6688 of 21 Chaoual 1439 (July 5, 2018),
p.1384;
- Law No. 27-14 relating to the fight against human trafficking
promulgated by Dahir No. 1 -16-127 of 21 Kaada 1437 (August 25, 2016);
Official Bulletin No. 6526 of 15 Rabii I 1438 (December 15, 2016), p.1952;
- Law No. 73-15 modifying and supplementing certain provisions of
penal code promulgated by dahir n° 1 -16-104 of 13 chaoual 1437 (18
July 2016);Official Bulletin No. 6522 of 1st Rabii I 1438 (December 1st
2016), p.1860;
- Law No. 86-14 modifying and supplementing certain provisions of
Penal Code and criminal procedure relating to the fight against
terrorism promulgated by Dahir No. 1 -15-53 of 1st Shaabane 1436 (20

PRAISE TO GOD ALONE!
(Great Seal of H.M. Hassan II)
Let it be hereby known - may
e God will raise and strengthen
the content!
May Our Majesty Cherifian,
HAS DECIDED AS FOLLOWS:
Article 1
The text forming the penal code as published in
annex to this dahir.
Section 2
The provisions of this code will be applied throughout
the extent of the Kingdom as of June 17, 1963.
However, those of these provisions relating to judicial placement
in a therapeutic establishment and to judicial placement in a
agricultural colony, personal security measures provided for by articles
80 to 85 of the said code, will only receive application when their implementation
force will have been specially decided by joint decrees of the
various interested ministers.

2 - Official Bulletin No. 2640 bis of 12 Moharrem 1383 (June 5, 1963), p.843.

- 7 - Article 3
Courts and tribunals will continue to observe the laws and regulations
individuals governing all matters not regulated by the code.
However, these courts will only be able to impose penalties
falling into the categories provided for by him and according to the distinctions
decreed in article 5 below.
Article 4
The provisions of this code apply even to regulated matters
by specific laws and regulations in everything that is not in these laws
is subject to express provisions.
Article 5
Penalties imposed by decisions that have become irrevocable and are ongoing
of execution on the date of entry into force of this code or which must be
suffered after this date of entry into force, will be so
which it follows:
If the sentence imposed is a custodial sentence of a duration
less than one month, it will be suffered as detention under the conditions
provided for in article 29 of the code;
If the sentence imposed is a custodial sentence of a duration
from one month to five years or a custodial sentence of more than five
years sanctioning a criminal act, due to the state of recid ive of the
convicted, it will be suffered as imprisonment under the conditions
provided for in section 28;
If the sentence imposed is a custodial sentence of a duration
greater than five years punishing a criminal act, it will be suffered
as imprisonment under the conditions provided for in article 24.
Article 6
In all cases where a sentence of an accessory penalty or
complementary order has been pronounced, and has not yet been executed or
found in progress, it will be automatically replaced by the
corresponding security measure: in particular judicial internment
provided for by articles 16 and 21 of the dahir of 15 Safar 1373 (October 24, 1953)
forming the Moroccan penal code, and by the dahir of 5 Joumada I 1352 (28
August 1933) relating to the repression of repeat offenses by the High Court

- 8 - Cherifien, will be replaced by the relegation referred to in articles 63 to 69 of
code attached.
Article 7
Courts regularly seized of offenses which, under the terms of the
code approved by this dahir are no longer within their jurisdiction
however, remain competent to judge these offenses if their referral
results from a referral order or summons prior to the
date of entry into force of this code.
In all other cases the procedures will be transferred without further notice.
formality to the competent court.
However, the applicable penalties will be those in force at the time.
where the offense was committed unless the attached code has enacted
a softer penalty which will then have to be applied.
Article 8
Are repealed from the date of application of the attached code
all legal provisions to the contrary, and in particular:
the dahir of 9 Ramadan 1331 (August 12, 1913) making it applicable to
Morocco the French penal code, as well as the later dahirs having
introduced texts which supplemented or modified this code;
the dahir of 16 safar 1373 (24 October 1953) forming the penal code
Moroccan, the dahir of 16 rebia II 1373 (December 23, 1953) modifying and
completing the previous one, as well as all other dahirs having completed them
or modified;
the dahir of 6 rejeb 1332 (June 1, 1914) implementing the code
criminal court of the former northern zone of Morocco, as well as all dahirs having completed
or modified this code;
the dahir of 19 Joumada II 1343 (January 15, 1925) bearing
promulgation of the “penal code” in the Tangier area, as well as all
dahirs having completed or modified the latter;
the dahir of 6 Moharrem 1362 (January 12, 1943) making applicable the
law of July 23, 1942, relating to family abandonment;
the dahir of 30 Rebia I 1379 (October 3, 1959) repressing the abandonment of
family;

- 9 - the Khalifian dahir of June 17, 1942 relating to the abandonment of family in
the former northern zone of the Kingdom.
References to the provisions of the texts repealed hereby
dahir, contained in legislative or regulatory texts,
applies
ent to the corresponding provisions decreed by the code herein -
annexed.
Section 9
Article 490 of the dahir of 1st Shaabane 1378 (February 10, 1959)
forming the criminal procedure code is repealed and replaced by the
following provision3:
"Article 490. - When it emerges from the debates that the accused was at the
time of the facts, or is currently suffering from disorders of his faculties
mental, the criminal court applies, depending on the case, the articles
76, 78 or 79 of the penal code."

Done in Rabat, on 28 Joumada II 1382 (November 26, 1962).

- 11 - CCOODDEE PPEENNAALL
DDIISSPPOOSSIITTIIOONNSS PPRREELLIIMMIINNAAIIRREESS
(Articles 1 to 12)
Article 1
The criminal law determines and constitutes offenses the acts of
the man who, because of the social unrest they cause, justifies
the application of penalties or security measures to their perpetrator.
Section 2
No one can cite ignorance of criminal law as an excuse.
Section 3
No one can be condemned for an act which is not expressly
provided for as an offense by law, nor punished with penalties that the law does not have
enacted.
Article 4
No one can be convicted for an act which, according to the law in force
at the time it was committed, did not constitute an offence.
Article 5
No one can be condemned for an act which, by the operation of a law
subsequent to its commission, no longer constitutes an offense;if a
conviction has been pronounced, the execution of the sentences is terminated as long as
main and accessories.
Article 6
When several laws have been in force between the time when
the offense has been committed and the final judgment, the law, whose
provisions are the least rigorous, must be applied.
Article 7
The provisions of articles 5 and 6 above do not concern
temporary laws.These, even after they have ceased to be in

- 12 - force, continue to govern offenses committed during the duration of
their application.
Article 8
No security measure may be imposed except in cases and
conditions provided for by law.
The applicable security measures are those decreed by law in
in force at the time of judgment of the offense.
Section 9
The execution of a security measure ceases when the event which caused it
motivated no longer constitutes an offense by the effect of a subsequent law
or when this security measure is itself removed by law.
Article 10
Are subject to Moroccan criminal law, all those who, nationals,
foreigners or stateless persons, are in the territory of the Kingdom, except
exceptions established by domestic public law or international law.
Article 11
Are considered to be part of the territory, ships or vessels
Moroccan aircraft wherever they are, unless they
are subject, under international law, to foreign law.
Article 12
Moroccan criminal law applies to offenses committed outside
of the Kingdom when they fall within the jurisdiction of the courts
Moroccan repressive measures under the provisions of articles 751 to 756
of the criminal procedure code4.

4 - Articles 707 to 712 of Law No. 22.01 relating to the aforementioned criminal procedure.

- 13 - LLIIVVRREE PPRREEMMIIEERR DDEESS PPEEIINNEESS EETT DDEESS MMEESSUURREESS DDEE
SSUURREETTEE
(Articles 13 to 109)
Section 13
The penalties and security measures set out in this code are
applicable to adults over the age of eighteen Gregorian years.
Special rules apply to juvenile delinquents
provided for in Book III of the law relating to criminal procedure5.
TTIITTRREE PPRREEMMIIEERR DDEESS PPEEIINNEESS
(Articles 14 to 60)
Article 14
The penalties are principal or accessory.
They are principal when they can be pronounced without being
added to no other penalty.
They are incidental when they cannot be inflicted
separately or that they are the consequences of a main sentence.






5 - Article modified by article 1 of law no. 24.03 modifying and supplementing the code
penal, promulgated by Dahir No. 1 -03-207 of Ramadan 16, 1424 (November 11, 2003),
Official Bulletin No. 5178 of 22 kaada 1424 (January 15, 200
4), p.114.

- 14 - CCHHAAPPIITTRREE PPRREEMMIIEERR DDEESS PPEEIINNEESS PPRRIINNCCIIPPAALLEESS
(Articles 15 to 35)
Article 15
The main penalties are: criminal, misdemeanor or
contraventions.
Article 16
The main criminal penalties are:
1° Death;
2° Perpetual reclusion;
3° Temporary imprisonment for a period of five to thirty years;
4° Forced residence;
5° Civic degradation.
Section 17
The main criminal penalties are:
1 - Imprisonment;
2 - The fine of more than 1,200 dirhams6.
The duration of the prison sentence is at least one month and
of five years at most, except in cases of repeat offenses or other cases where the law
determines other limits.
Article 18
The main criminal penalties are:
1 - Detention of less than one month;
2 - The fine of 30 dirhams to 1,200 dirhams7.

6 - Paragraph amended by article 1 r of law no. 3 -80 modifying certain provisions of
penal code promulgated by dahir n° 1 -81-283 of 11 rejeb 1402 (May 6, 1982), Bulletin
Official No. 3636 of Ramadan 15, 1402 (July 7, 1982), p.351, then by Law No. 25 -93
amending the penal code promulgated by Dahir No. 1 -94-284 of Safar 15, 1415 (July 25
1994), Official Bulletin No. 4266 of 24 Safar 1415 (August 3, 1994), p.371.
7 - Paragraph modified by article 1 of law no. 3 -80 modifying certain provisions of
penal code, then by the single article of law no. 25-93 amending the aforementioned penal code.

- 15 - Articles 19 to 238
Article 24
The sentence of reclusiveness is carried out in a central house with
nighttime isolation whenever the layout of the premises allows it
and with compulsory work, except in the case of proven physical incapacity.
Under no circumstances may a person sentenced to imprisonment be admitted to
outside work before having served ten years of his sentence if he was
sentenced to life imprisonment or a quarter of the sentence imposed if he was
sentenced on time9.
Section 25
Forced residence consists of the assignment to the convicted person of a
place of residence or a specific area, of which he cannot
leave without authorization for the period fixed by the decision.This
duration cannot be less than five years, when it is pronounced as
main penalty.
The decision to sentence to forced residence is notified to the
general directorate of national security which must carry out the control of
this residence.
If necessary, a temporary travel authorization to
within the territory may be issued by the Minister of Justice.
Article 26
Civic degradation consists of:
1° In the dismissal and exclusion of the condemned from all
public functions and all public employment or offices;
2° In the deprivation of the right to be a voter or eligible and, in
general, of all civil and political rights and the right to carry
any decoration;

8 - Articles 19 to 23 of the penal code were repealed by article 756 of law no. 22 -01
relating to the aforementioned criminal procedure.Their provisions have been inserted in articles 601
to 607 of Law No. 22-01 relating to the aforementioned criminal procedure.
9 - See law no. 23-98 relating to the organization and operation of establishments
penitentiaries promulgated by Dahir No. 1 -99-200 of 13 Joumada I 1420 (August 25, 1999),
Official Bulletin No. 4726 of 5 Joumada II 1420 (September 16, 1999), p 715.

- 16 - 3° Unable to be a jury assessor, expert, to serve as a witness
in all acts and to file in court other than to give
simple information;
4° In the incapacity to be guardian or subrogated guardian, except for his
own children;
5° In the deprivation of the right to bear arms, to serve in
the army, to teach, to run a school or to be employed in a
educational establishment as a professor, master or supervisor.
Civic degradation, when it constitutes a principal penalty,
is, unless otherwise specifically provided, pronounced for a period of
two to ten years.
Section 27
Whenever civic degradation is pronounced as
main penalty, it can be accompanied by imprisonment of which
the duration must be fixed by the sentencing decision without ever
may exceed five years.
When civic degradation cannot be inflicted because the
guilty is a Moroccan who has already lost his civil rights, or a
foreigner, the applicable penalty is imprisonment for five to ten years.
Section 28
The sentence of imprisonment is served in one of the
establishments intended for this or in a special area of a house
central, with compulsory work inside or outside, except in the case
of noted physical incapacity.
Article
29
The sentence of detention is served in civil prisons or in
their annexes, with compulsory work inside or outside, outside the
case of noted physical incapacity.
Article 30
The duration of any custodial sentence is calculated from the
day on which the convicted person is detained under the decision which has become
irrevocable.
When there has been preventive detention, it is entirely
deducted from the length of the sentence and is calculated from the day on which the

- 17 - convicted person was either kept in custody or placed under court order for
the offense leading to the conviction.
The duration of custodial sentences is calculated as follows:
When the sentence imposed is one day, its duration is 24 hours;
When it is less than a month, it is counted in days
full 24 hours;
When the sentence imposed is one month, its duration is thirty
days;
The sentence of more than one month is calculated from date to date.
Article 31
When several custodial sentences must be served, the
convicted person carries out the most serious sentence first, unless the law
does not provide otherwise.
Article 32
If it is verified that a woman sentenced to a custodial sentence of
liberty is more than six months pregnant, she will only suffer her sentence
forty days after its delivery.If she is already incarcerated, she
will benefit, for the necessary time, from the detention regime
preventive.
The execution of custodial sentences is deferred for
women who gave birth less than forty days before their
conviction.
Article 33
Husband and wife convicted, even for offenses
different, to a prison sentence of less than one year and not
detained on the day of judgment, do not simultaneously serve their sentence,
if, with proof of a certain domicile, they are responsible for and under their
protection, a child under eighteen who cannot be taken in
under satisfactory conditions by any public person or
private unless otherwise requested by them.
When the prison sentence pronounced against each of the
spouse is more than one year, and if they are dependent on them or under their
protection of a child under eighteen years of age or if the child cannot be
collected by members of his family or by a public person or

- 18 - private, under satisfactory conditions, the provisions of the law
relating to criminal procedure on the protection of children in situations
difficult10, or the provisions of the kafala for abandoned children11,
when the related conditions are met, are then applicable12.
Section 34
When there was preventive detention and only a sentence
fine is imposed, the judge may, by decision specially
reasoned, exempt the convicted person from all or part of this fine.
Article 35
The fine consists of the obligation, for the convicted person, to pay
profit of the Treasury, a determined sum of money, counted in currency
legal tender in the Kingdom.

10 - See the provisions on the protection of children in difficult situations provided for in the
Articles 512 to 517 of Law 22.01 relating to the aforementioned criminal procedure.
11 - The first article of Law No. 15-01 relating to the care (kafala) of children
abandoned promulgated by Dahir No. 1 -02-172 of 1st Rabii II 1423 (June 13, 2002), Bulletin
Official No. 5036 of 25 Jumada 1423 (September 5, 2002), p.914, provides that “Is considered
as abandoned child any child of either sex who has not reached the age of 18
Gregorian years completed when he finds himself in one of the following situations:
- being born to unknown parents or an unknown father and a known mother who abandoned him
his own free will;
- be an orphan or have parents unable to provide for their needs or who do not have
legal means of subsistence;
- have bad parents who do not assume their responsibility for protection and
of orientation with a view to leading him on the right path, as when they are deprived of
legal guardianship or that one of the two, after the death or incapacity of the other, turns out to be misguided
and does not fulfill his above-mentioned duty towards the child.»
Article 2 of the same law provides that: “The care (kafala) of a child
abandoned, within the meaning of this law, is the commitment to take charge of the protection,
the education and maintenance of an abandoned child in the same way as a father would do for his
child.The kafala does not give any right to filiation or inheritance.»
12 - Article modified and supplemented by article 3 of law no. 24-03 modifying and supplementing the
aforementioned penal code e.

- 19 -
CCHHAAPPIITTRREE IIII DDEESS PPEEIINNEESS AACCCCEESSSSSOOIIRREESS
(Articles 36 to 48
)
Article 36
The accessory penalties are:
1° Legal prohibition;
2° Civic degradation;
3° The suspension of the exercise of certain civic, civil or
of family;
4° Loss or suspension of the right to pensions provided by the State
and public establishments.
However, this loss cannot apply to persons responsible for
support for one or more children, subject to the provisions
provided for in this regard by pension schemes13.
5° Partial confiscation of property belonging to the convicted person,
regardless of the confiscation provided as a security measure by
section 89;
6° The dissolution of a legal entity;
7° Publication of the sentencing decision.
Article 37
Legal prohibition and civic degradation when it is
accessory, only attach to criminal penalties.
They do not have to be pronounced and apply automatically.
Article 38
The legal ban deprives the convicted person of the exercise of his rights
assets during the execution of the main sentence.
However, he always has the right to choose an agent for the
represent in the exercise of his rights, under the supervision of the designated guardian
in accordance with the requirements of the article below.

13 - Article supplemented by article 2 of Law No. 24-03 cited above e.

- 22 - Article 39
It is carried out, in the forms provided for prohibited
judicial14, to the appointment of a guardian to control the management of
property of the convict prohibited legal.If the latter has chosen a representative
to administer his property, it will remain under the control of the guardian and
will be responsible to him.Otherwise, the tutor will take care of
personally from this administration.
During the term of the sentence, he cannot be handed over to the legal ban
no sum derived from his income, except for cause
of food and within the limits authorized by the administration
penitentiary.
The property of the interdicted person is returned to him at the end of his sentence and the
guardian reports to him on his administration.
Article 40
When imposing a criminal sentence, the courts may,
in the cases determined by law and for a period of one to ten years,
prohibit the convicted person from exercising one or more of the rights
civic, civil or family members referred to in Article 26.
Courts may also apply the provisions of
first paragraph of this article when pronouncing a sentence
tort for a terrorism offense15.

The definitive loss of the pension provided by the State attaches to any
sentenced to death or life imprisonment.She doesn't have
not to be pronounced and applies automatically.

in the previous paragraph may be removed from the suspension of pension rights
for the duration of the sentence.

- 21 - Article 42
Confiscation consists of the attribution to the State of a fraction of the
property of the convicted person or certain of his specially designated property.
Section 43
In the event of conviction for an act classified as a crime, the judge may
order confiscation, for the benefit of the State, subject to the rights of
third parties, objects and things which were used or were to be used in the offense,
or which are the products thereof, as well as donations or other advantages which
were used or were intended to be used to reward the perpetrator of the offense.
Section 44
In the event of conviction for acts classified as misdemeanors or
contraventions, the judge can only order confiscation in cases
expressly provided for by law.
Article 44 -116
When it concerns an act constituting a terrorism offense, the
court may order the confiscation provided for in article 42 of this
code.
Confiscation must always be pronounced, in the cases provided for in the
articles 43 and 44 of this code, subject to the rights of third parties, in the event
conviction for a terrorism offense.
Section 45
Except for the exceptions provided for by this code, confiscation does not
applies only to property belonging to the convicted person.
If the convicted person is co-owner
ire of undivided property, confiscation does not
relates only to its share and automatically entails sharing or licitation.
Section 46
The alienation of confiscated property is pursued by the administration
domains in the forms prescribed for the sale of State property.

aforementioned.

- 22 - The property vested in the State as a result of the confiscation remains
encumbered, up to their value, of legitimate debts
prior to the conviction.
Section 47
The dissolution of a legal person consists of the prohibition
to continue the social activity, even under another name and with others
directors, administrators or managers.It leads to the liquidation of
property of the legal entity.
It can only be pronounced in cases provided for by law and in
under an express provision of the sentencing decision.
Section 48
In cases determined by law, the trial court may
order that his sentencing decision be published in full
or by extracts from one or more newspapers that it designates or will be
posted in the places it indicates, all at the expense of the convicted person,
without however the publication costs being able to exceed the sum
fixed for this purpose by the sentencing decision, nor that the duration of
the display may exceed one month.

(Articles 49 to 60)
Article 49
Every condemned person must fully bear the penalties pronounced against
him, unless one of the causes of extinction, exemption
or suspension below:
1° The death of the condemned person;
2° Amnesty;
3° The repeal of the criminal law;
4° Grace;
5° Prescription;
6° Suspension of execution of the sentence;

- 23 - 7° Conditional release on;
8° The transaction when the law expressly provides for it.
Article 50
The death of the condemned person does not prevent the execution of
monetary judgments on property from his estate.
Article 51
Amnesty can only result from an express provision of the law.
This determines the effects, subject however to the rights of the
third party.
Article 52
Except in the case provided for in article 7 for the application of laws
temporary, the repeal of the criminal law hinders the execution of the
sentence not yet served and puts an end to the current execution.
Article 53
The right of pardon is an attribute of the Sovereign.
It is exercised under the conditions set by dahir n°1-57-387 of 16
rejeb 1377 (February 6, 1958) relating to graces17.
In matters of offenses and contraventions, when an appeal for pardon is
formed in favor of a detained convict, the release of this convict
may, exceptionally, be ordered by the Minister of Justice
until the request for pardon has been decided.
Article 54
The prescription of the sentence removes the condemned person from the effects of the
conviction under the conditions provided for in articles 688 to 693 of the code
of criminal procedure18.
Article 55
In the event of a sentence of imprisonment or a fine,
contravention, if the accused has not suffered a previous conviction

17- Official Bulletin No. 2365 of February 21, 1958, p.359.
18 - Articles 648 to 653 of Law No. 22.01 relating to the aforementioned criminal procedure.

- 24 - to imprisonment for a crime or offense under common law, the jurisdiction
judgment may, by a reasoned provision of its decision, order
that the execution of the sentence will be suspended.
Article 56
The conviction will be deemed void if, for a period of
five years from the day on which the judgment or decision granting the
suspended sentence has become irrevocable, the condemned person does not commit any crime or
common law offense which gives rise to a sentence of
imprisonment or a more serious penalty.
If, on the contrary, he commits such a crime or offense within the period of five
years provided for in the preceding paragraph, the sentence of imprisonment or
a more serious penalty punishing this crime or offense, even if it
intervenes only after the expiration of the said period, entails automatically, from
that it has become irrevocable, the revocation of the suspended sentence.
The first sentence is then executed before the second without
possibility of confusion with the latter.
Article 57
The stay granted has no effect on the payment of the costs of the trial and
civil reparations.It does not extend either to accessory penalties or to
disabilities resulting from the conviction.
However, these accessory penalties and these incapacities cease fully
law of the day when, by application of the provisions of the first paragraph
of
the preceding article, the conviction is deemed void.
Section 58
When the convicted person is present at the hearing, the president of the
court must, immediately after delivery of the decision
granting the suspended sentence, warn him that in the event of a new conviction within the
conditions provided for in article 56, he must carry out the sentence without confusion
possible with that subsequently inflicted and that he will incur
possibly increased penalties for repeat offenses.
Section 59
Conditional release benefits the convicted person, due to
his good conduct in the penitentiary establishment, an implementation
anticipated freedom, on condition that he behave honestly in the future

- 25 - and under the condition that he will be reincarcerated to serve the remainder of his
penalty in the event of duly noted misconduct or non-compliance
conditions set by the conditional release decision.
It is governed by the provisions of articles 663 to 672 of the code of
criminal procedure19.
Article 60
Rehabilitation is not a cause of extinction, exemption or
suspension of sentence;it only erases for the future and in the
conditions provided for in articles 730 to 747 of the code of criminal procedure20,
the effects of the conviction and the resulting incapacities.

convicted in the above-mentioned places constitutes a danger to public order

Section 75
Judicial internment in a psychiatric establishment
consists of placement in an appropriate establishment, by decision
of a court of judgment, of an individual presumed author, co-author
or accessory to a crime or misdemeanor, who due to the disturbances of his
mental faculties existing during the facts attributed to him, and noted
by medical expertise, must be declared totally irresponsible and
is thus exempt from the possible application of the penalties provided for by
the law.
Article 76
When a trial court considers, after medical expertise,
that the individual referred to him under the charge of crime or the
prevention of crime, was totally irresponsible due to unrest
mental health existing at the time of the acts attributed to her, she must:
1° Establish that the accused or the accused was present at the time of the
made in the impossibility of understanding or wanting, as a result of
disorders of his mental faculties;
2° Declare him totally irresponsible and pronounce his absolution;
3° Order, if the troubles persist, his internment in a
psychiatric establishment.
The validity of the detention permit is extended until internment
effective.
Section 77
Judicial internment continues for as long as required
public security and the healing of the internee.
The internee must initially be placed under observation.He
must be examined whenever the psychiatrist requires it as necessary, and in
in any case every six months.
When the treating psychiatrist considers it necessary to terminate
judicial internment, he must inform the head of the general prosecutor's office of

- 31 - the court of appeal which may, within ten days from the
receipt of this notice, appeal against the exit decision, within
the conditions set by article 28 of the dahir of 21 chaoual 1378 relating to
prevention and treatment of mental illnesses and protection
mentally ill27.This appeal is suspensive.
Article 78
When a trial court considers, after expert assessment
medical, that the author of a crime or an offense, although able to ensure
his defense during the debates, was nevertheless affected during the facts which
are attributed to him for a weakening of his mental faculties resulting in
a partial reduction of its liability, it must:
1° Find that the facts pursued are attributable to the accused or to the
warned;
2° Declare him partially irresponsible due to
the weakening of his mental faculties at the time of the events;
3° Pronounce the sentence;
4° Order, if necessary, that the condemned person will be hospitalized in a
psychiatric establishment, prior to the execution of any sentence
deprivation of liberty.Hospitalization is deducted from the duration of this
sentence, and ends under the conditions provided for in the last paragraph of
section 77.
Article 79
When a trial court considers, after expert assessment
medical, that the individual who is referred to him under the accusation of crime or
crime prevention was responsible in whole or in part at the
time of the facts attributed to him, but that due to disturbances of
his mental faculties occurring or worsening subsequently, he finds himself
Unable to defend itself during the debates, it must:
1° Establish that the accused or the accused is incapable of
to defend, as a result of the present alteration of his mental faculties;
2° Stay of proceedings;

psychiatric.

Section 80
Judicial placement in a therapeutic establishment
consists of being placed under surveillance in an appropriate establishment,
p
by decision of a court of law, of an individual, author,
co-author or accomplice either of a crime, of a criminal offense or of
police, suffering from chronic intoxication caused by alcohol or
narcotics, when the criminality of the perpetrator appears linked
to this intoxication.
Section 81
When a trial court considers it necessary to apply
of the provisions of the preceding article, it must:
1° Declare that the act pursued is attributable to the accused or the
warned;
2° Expressly note that the criminality of the author of
the offense appears to be linked to chronic intoxication caused by alcohol
or narcotics;
3° Pronounce the sentence;
4° Order, in addition, judicial placement in an establishment
therapeutic for a duration which may not exceed two years.
The convicted person will be subject to the placement measure, previously
to the execution of the sentence, unless the court decides
otherwise.

- 33 - Article 82
The measure of judicial placement in an establishment
Therapeutic treatment is revoked when it is found that the causes which
had caused it have disappeared.
When the head physician of the therapeutic establishment considers
having to put an end to this measure, he informs the head of the general public prosecutor's office
of the court of appeal which, within ten days after receipt of this
opinion, may appeal against the decision, under the conditions
established by article 77.
Article 83
Judicial placement in an agricultural colony consists of
the obligation imposed by the decision of the trial court, on a
convicted of a crime or any legally punishable offense
of imprisonment, to stay in a specialized center where he will be
employed in agricultural work, when the criminality of this convict
appears linked to habits of idleness, or that it has been established that it draws
usually its resources from illegal activities.
Section 84
When a trial court considers it necessary to apply
of the provisions of the preceding article, it must:
1° Declare that the act under investigation is attributable to the accused or the
warned;
2° Expressly note that this fact is linked to habits of idleness
of the condemned or it is established that he usually draws his
resources of illegal activities;
3° Pronounce the sentence;
4° Orders, in addition, the judicial placement in a colony
agricultural for a period which cannot be less than six months, nor
greater than two years.
The stay in the agricultural colony immediately follows the execution of
the punishment.
Section 85
The judicial placement measure provided for in article 83 is revoked
when the conduct of the condemned person gives rise to his amendment.

- 34 - The decision of revocation is taken, on the proposal of the director of
the agricultural colony, by the trial court which had ordered it.
When the placement has been ordered by a criminal court, the
criminal court which was called upon to constitute this criminal court
is competent to pronounce the revocation.
Article 86
The inability to exercise any public functions or employment must be
pronounced by the court in cases prescribed by law and when it
This is an offense constituting an act of terrorism28.
Apart from these cases, it may be, when the court finds
and declares, by an express provision of the decision, that the offense
committed has a direct relationship with the exercise of the function or
employment and that it reveals in its author a moral perversity
incompatible with the normal exercise of the function or employment.
Unless the law provides otherwise, this incapacity is
pronounced for a period which cannot exceed ten years, from
day on which the sentence was suffered.
Article 87
The ban on exercising a profession, activity or art must be
pronounced against those convicted of crime or misdemeanor, when the
court finds that the offense committed has a direct relationship with
the exercise of the profession, activity or art, and there are serious fears
that by continuing to exercise them, the condemned person is a danger to the
public security, health, morality or savings.
This ban is pronounced for a period which cannot
exceed ten years, from the day on which the sentence was served, except in cases where
the law provides otherwise.
The provisional execution of this measure may be ordered by the
decision of conviction, notwithstanding the exercise of all means of
ordinary or extraordinary appeals.

CCHHAAPPIITTRREE IIII DDEESS CCAAUUSSEESS DD’’EEXXTTIINNCCTTIIOONN,, DD’’EEXXEEMMPPTTIIOONN
OOUU DDEE SSUUSSPPEENNSSSIIOONN DDEESS MMEESSUURREESS DDEE SAFETY
(Articles 93 to 104)
Section 93
Subject to the provisions of articles 103 and 104, the causes
extinction, exemption or suspension of security measures are:
1° The death of the condemned person;
2° Amnesty;

- 38 - 3° The repeal of the criminal law;
4° Grace;
5° Prescription;
6° Conditional release;
7° Rehabilitation;
8° The transaction, when the law expressly provides for it.
The suspension of the execution of the sentence has no effect on the measures of
safety.
Section 94
The death of the condemned person does not prevent the execution of the
real security measures.
Section 95
The law providing amnesty for the offense or the principal penalty, to
unless it decides otherwise by an express provision, stops
the execution of personal security measures and remains without effect on
actual security measures.
Section 96
The repeal of the criminal law puts an end to the execution of measures of
security under the conditions provided for in Article 9.
Section 97
Remission by pardon of the main sentence does not extend to
security measures only if it is expressly decided by the
decision which grants it.
Section 98
Prescription of the main penalty does not entail prescription
security measures.
Section 99
A security measure that remains unexecuted is prescribed by a
duration of five years from the expiration of the custodial sentence
freedom actually suffered, or payment of the fine, or from the day on which
the statute of limitations on the sentence is acquired.

- 39 - However, when the security measure had been ordered for a
duration of more than five years, the prescription is only acquired upon expiry
of equal duration.
Article 100
The provisions of articles 98 and 99 are not applicable to
the ban on residence only subject to the rules laid down by article
689 of the Code of Criminal Procedure and 73, paragraph 2 of this Code30.
Article 101
The decision pronouncing conditional release may suspend
execution of security measures.
Article 102
The rehabilitation of the convicted person pronounced under the conditions
provided for in articles 730 to 747 of the code of criminal procedure31 puts an end to
the execution of security measures.
Article 103
Causes for termination, exemption or suspension of measures
of security, other than death, do not apply to internment
judicial in a psychiatric establishment and judicial placement
in a therapeutic establishment.
These two security measures end under the conditions set
by articles 78 and 82.
Article 104
The forfeiture of paternal rights obeys the rules
extinction, exemption or suspension specific to it.

31 - Articles 687 to 703 of Law No. 22.01 relating to the aforementioned criminal procedure.

(Articles 105 to 109)
Section 105
Any judgment or judgment pronouncing a penalty or a measure of
security must rule on the costs and expenses of the trial, under the conditions
provided for in articles 347 and 349 of the code of criminal procedure32.
It also rules, if necessary, on restitutions and the allocation of
damages.
Article 106
Restitution consists of the return to their legitimate owner
objects, sums, movable effects, placed under the control of justice
the occasion for the prosecution of an offense.
This restitution may be ordered by the court, even if the
owner does not intervene in the debates.
Article 107
At the request of the victim of the offense, the court may, in
furthermore, by a specially reasoned provision, order restitution:
1° Amounts from the sale of objects or movable effects
which should have been returned in kind;
2° Subject to the rights of third parties, objects or movable effects
obtained with the proceeds of the infringement.
Article 108
The award of damages must ensure that the victim is
full compensation for the personal, current and certain harm suffered by him
directly caused by the offense.
Section 109
All individuals convicted of the same crime, the same offense
or the same contravention are, if the judge does not
decides otherwise, required

32 - Articles 365 to 367 of Law No. 22.01 relating to the aforementioned criminal procedure.

- 41 - jointly with fines, restitution, damages and
fees.

TTIITTRREE PPRREEMMIIEERR DDEE LL''IINNFFRRAACCTTIIOONN
(Articles 110 to 125)
Article 110
The offense is an act or abstention contrary to criminal law and
repressed by her.
CCHHAAPPIITTRREE PPRREEMMIIEERR DDEESS DDIIVVEERRSSEESS CCAATTEEGGOORRIIEESS
DD’’IINNFFRRAACCTTIIOONNSS
(Articles 111 to 113)
Section 111
The offenses are classified as a crime, misdemeanor, misdemeanor
police or ticket:
The offense that the law punishes with one of the penalties provided for in article 16
is a crime;
The offense that the law punishes with a prison sentence of which it
setting the maximum at more than two years is a misdemeanor;
The offense that the law punishes with a prison sentence of which it
sets the maximum at two years or less than two years, or a fine of
more than 200 dirhams33 is a police offense;
The offense that the law punishes with one of the penalties provided for in article 18
is a violation.

33 - The minimum fine for criminal offenses was increased to 200 dirhams by article 2 of law no.
3-80 cited above.

- 43 - Article 112
The category of the offense is not modified when, as a result
a cause for mitigating the sentence or due to recidivism
of the convicted person, the judge pronounces a sentence relating to another category
of infringement.
Article 113
The category of the offense is modified when due to
aggravating circumstances, the law establishes a penalty relating to another
category of offense.
CCHHAAPPIITTRREE IIII DDEE LLAA TTEENNTTAATTIIVVEE
(Articles 114 to 117)
Article 114
Any attempted crime that was manifested by a
commencement of execution or by unequivocal acts tending
directly to commit it, if it has not been suspended or if it has not
missed its effect only by circumstances beyond the control
of its author, is assimilated to the consummate crime and repressed as such.
Article 115
Attempted crime is only punishable under a provision
special of the law.
Section 116
Attempted contravention is never punishable.
Article 117
The attempt is punishable even though the desired aim is not
could be reached due to a factual circumstance unknown to
the author.

- 44 -
CCHHAAPPIITTRREE IIIIII DDUU CCOONNCCOOUURRSS DD’’IINNFFRRAACCTTIIOONNSS
(Articles 118 to 123)
Article 118
The single fact capable of several qualifications must be
appreciated according to the most serious of them.
Section 119
The simultaneous or successive commission of more than one offense
not separated by an irrevocable conviction constitutes the competition
of infractions.
Section 120
In the event of a combination of several crimes or offenses referred
simultaneously in the same court, a single sentence is pronounced
deprivation of liberty the duration of which cannot exceed the maximum of that
enacted by law for the repression of the most serious offense.
When due to a plurality of prosecutions, several penalties
custodial sentences have been imposed, only the harshest sentence is
executed.
However, if the sentences handed down are of the same nature, the judge
may, by reasoned decision, order the accumulation in whole or in part,
within the limit of the maximum prescribed by law for the most serious offense
serious.
Section 121
Monetary penalties, whether principal or incidental to
a custodial sentence is cumulative, unless the judge decides
decides otherwise by an express provision.
Section 122
In the event of a combination of several crimes or misdemeanors, the penalties
accessories and security measures are cumulative, unless the judge decides
decides otherwise by a reasoned provision.
Security measures whose nature does not permit execution
simultaneous execution are executed in the order provided for in section 91.

- 45 - Article 123
In matters of contraventions, the accumulation of sentences is obligatory.
CCHHAAPPIITTRREE IIVV DDEESS FFAAIITTSS JJUUSSTTIIFFIICCAATTIIFFSS QQUUII
SSUUPPPPRRIIMMEENNTT LL’IINNFFRRAACCTTIIOONN
(Articles 124 and 125)
Section 124
There is no crime, misdemeanor or contravention:
1° When the act was ordered by law and ordered by authority
legitimate; legitimate;
2° When the author was materially forced to perform or was
materially placed in the impossibility of avoiding the infringement, by a
event coming from a foreign cause which he could not resist;
3° When the infringement was required by the current necessity of
self-defense of oneself or of others or of property belonging to
oneself or others, provided that the defense is proportionate to the
seriousness of the attack.
Article 125
Are presumed accomplished in a case of current necessity of
self-defense:
1° The homicide committed, the injuries caused or the blows carried out, in
preventing, during the night, climbing or breaking into fences, walls
or entrance to a house or inhabited apartment or their
outbuildings;
2° The offense committed while defending oneself or others against
the author of violent theft or looting.

- 46 - TTIITTRREE IIII DDEE LL'AAUUTTEEUURR DDEE LL'IINNFFRRAACCTTIIOONN ::
(Articles 126 to 162)
Article 126
The penalties and security measures decreed by this code are
applicable to natural persons.
Article 127
Legal entities can only be sentenced to penalties
financial and accessory penalties provided for under numbers 5, 6 and 7
of article 36. They may also be subject to the measures of
real security of article 62.
CCHHAAPPIITTRREE PPRREEMMIIEERR DDEE LLAA PPAARRTTIICCIIPPAATTIIOONN DDEE
PPLLUUSSIIEEUURRSS PPEERRSSOONNNEESS AA LL’IINNFFRRAACCTTIIOONN
(Articles 128 to 131)
Article 128
All those who, personally, are considered co-authors
took part in the material execution of the offence.
Section 129
Are considered accomplices to an offense qualified as a crime
or offense those who, without direct participation in this offense, have:
1° By gifts, promises, threats, abuse of authority or power,
culpable machinations or artifices, provoked to this action or given
instructions for committing it;
2° Obtained weapons, instruments or any other means which will have
served in action knowing that they had to serve there;
3° With knowledge, helped or assisted the author or authors of
the action, in the facts which prepared or facilitated it;
4° With knowledge of their criminal conduct, usually
provided accommodation, place of retreat or meetings for one or more
criminals carrying out robbery or violence against the security of
the State, public peace, people or property.

- 47 - Complicity is never punishable in matters of contravention.
Section 130
The accomplice of a crime or misdemeanor is punishable by the penalty
repressing this crime or offense.
The personal circumstances from which aggravation results,
mitigation or exemption from punishment only has effect with regard to the sole
participant to which they relate.
The objective circumstances, inherent to the offense, which aggravate
or reduce the sentence, even if they are not known to everyone
who participated in this offense, have effect against them or in their
favor.
Section 131
The one who has determined a person not punishable because of a
condition or a personal quality, to commit an offense, is
liable to the penalties for the offense committed by that person.
CCHHAAPPIITTRREE IIII DDEE LLAA RREESSPPOOONNSSAABBIILLIITTEE PPEENNAALLEE
(Articles 132 to 140)
SECTION I RESPONSIBLE PERSONS
(Articles 132 and 133)

Article 132
Any person of sound mind and capable of discernment is
personally responsible:
Offenses she commits;
Crimes or offenses in which she is complicit;
Attempted crimes;
Attempts at certain crimes that she carries out under the conditions
provided for by law.

- 48 - This principle is only deviated from when the law provides otherwise.
Section 133
Crimes and misdemeanors are only punishable when they have been
committed intentionally.
Offenses committed recklessly are exceptionally
punishable in cases specially provided for by law.
Violations are punishable even when they have been
committed recklessly, except in cases where the law requires
expressly intends harm.
SECTION II OF MENTAL ALIEN ATION
(Articles 134 to 137)
Section 134
Anyone who, at the time of the
facts attributed to him, was due to disorders of his faculties
mental in the impossibility of understanding or wanting.
In matters of crime and misdemeanor, judicial internment in a
psychiatric establishment is ordered under the conditions provided for in
section 76.
In matters of contravention, the individual is absolved, if he is dangerous
for public order, is handed over to the administrative authority.
Section 135
A person is partially irresponsible who, at the time he committed
the offense, was suffering from a weakening of his faculties
mental disorders likely to reduce its co
misunderstanding or his will and
leading to a partial reduction of its liability.
In matters of crime and misdemeanor, application is made to the culprit
penalties or security measures provided for in Article 78.
In matters of contravention, the penalty is applied,
taking into account the mental state of the offender.

- 49 - Article 136
When an investigating court considers that an accused presents
manifest signs of mental insanity, she may, by decision
justified, order his temporary placement in an establishment
psychiatric with a view to placing him under observation and, if necessary, his
hospitalization under the conditions provided for by dahir n° l -58-295 of 21
chaoual 1378 (April 30, 1959) relating to the prevention and treatment of
mental illnesses and the protection of the mentally ill34.
The head of the general public prosecutor's office of the court of appeal must be notified by the
psychiatrist dealing with the discharge decision, at least ten days before
before it is executed.He may appeal against this decision.
under the conditions set by article 28 of the aforementioned dahir.This appeal will be
suspensive.
In the event of resumption of prosecution, and conviction of a sentence
deprivation of liberty, the trial court will have the power to impute
the duration of hospitalization over that of this sentence.
Article 13 7
Drunkenness, passionate or emotional states or those resulting from
the voluntary use of narcotic substances cannot, under any circumstances,
exclude or diminish liability.
The culprits can be placed in an institution
therapeutic in accordance with the provisions of Articles 80 and 81.
SECTION III CRIMINAL MINORITY
(Articles 138 to 140)
Section 138
A minor under the age of twelve is considered
criminally irresponsible for lack of discernment.
It can only be subject to the provisions of Book III of the law.
relating to criminal procedure35.

- 52 - Article 139
A minor of twelve years of age who has not reached eighteen years of age is,
criminally, considered partially irresponsible due to
of an insufficiency of discernment.
The minor benefits in the case provided for in the first paragraph of this
article of the minority excuse, and can only be the subject of
provisions of Book III of the law relating to criminal procedure36.
Article 140
Offenders who have reached the criminal age of eighteen years
gone, are deemed fully responsible37 38.
CCHHAAPPIITTRREE IIIIII DDEE LL’IINNDDIIVVIIDDUUAALLIISSAATTIIOONN DDEE LLAA PPEEIINNEE
(Articles 141 to 162)
Article 141
Within the limits of the maximum and minimum established by law
repressing the offense, the judge has discretionary power to
fix and individualize the sentence taking into account, on the one hand, the seriousness
of the offense committed, on the other hand, of the personality of the offender.
Section 142
The judge is required to impose a reduced sentence on the guilty party or
aggravated each time that one or more facts are proven
extenuating excuse, i.e. one or more aggravating circumstances
provided for by law.
He is required to pronounce absolution when proof is provided
of the existence in favor of the guilty party of an absolutory excuse provided for by
the law.

SECTION I LEGAL EXCUSES
(Articles 143 to 145)
Article 143
Excuses are facts restrictively determined by law which,
while allowing the offense and liability to remain, ensure that
delinquents either impunity when they are absolutory, or
moderation of the sentence when they are mitigating.
Article 144
Excuses are special and only apply to one or more
specific offenses.They are enacted by this code, in the
provisions of Book III concerning the various offenses.
Article 145
The absolutory excuse has the effect of providing the guilty party
the absolution which exempts him from the penalty, but leaves the judge the option of
apply absolutely personal or real security measures
other than relegation.
SECTION II OF THE GRANT BY THE CIRCUMSTANCES JUDGE
ATTACHMENTS
(Articles 146 to 151)
Article 146
When at the end of the debates the jurisdiction rep
resive seizure estimates
that, in the case submitted to it, the criminal sanction provided for by law
is excessive in relation either to the seriousness of the facts or to the guilt of
the author, it may, unless otherwise provided by law, grant the
condemned the benefit of mitigating circumstances.
The admission of mitigating circumstances is left to discretion.
of the judge, it is up to him to give special reasons for his decision on this

- 52 - point;the effects are exclusively personal and the penalty should not be
reduced only with regard to convicts who have been admitted to benefit from it.
This admission has the effect of leading, under the conditions
determined in the articles below, the reduction of the applicable penalties.
Article 147
If the penalty prescribed by law is death, the criminal court
applies the penalty of reclusion perpetua or imprisonment of
20 to 30 years old.
If the sentence imposed is that of reclusion perpetua, the court
criminal applies the penalty of imprisonment of 10 to 30 years.
If the sentence imposed is that of imprisonment of 20 to 30 years, the court
criminal applies the penalty of imprisonment of 5 to 20 years39.
If the minimum sentence imposed is ten years' imprisonment, the
criminal court applies imprisonment of five to ten years or a penalty
imprisonment of two to five years.
If the minimum sentence imposed is five years' imprisonment, the
criminal court applies a prison sentence of one to five
years 40.
If the criminal penalty imposed is accompanied by a fine, the
criminal court can reduce this to 120 dirhams41 or even the
delete.
When the penalty of imprisonment is substituted for a penalty
criminal, the criminal court may, in addition, impose a fine of
12,042 to 1,200 dirhams and, for a period of 5 to 10 years, the ban on
rights provided for in paragraphs 1 and 2 of article 26 and the stay ban.

If the sentence imposed is forced residence, the court pronounces the
civic degradation or imprisonment of six months to two years.
If the penalty imposed is civic degradation, the court pronounces

deprivation of certain of the rights provided for in article 26.

In matters of criminal offence, even in the event of a repeat offense, the judge,

only, may, when he notes the existence of circumstances

SECTION III AGG RAVANT CIRCUMSTANCES
(Articles 1 52 and 153)
Article 152
The increase in penalties applicable to certain offenses results
circumstances inherent either to the commission
sion of the offense, or at the
guilt of its author.
Section 153
The law determines these circumstances on the occasion of certain
criminal or misdemeanor offenses.
SECTION IV OF RECIPITION
(Articles 154 to 160)
Article 154
Is, under the conditions determined in the articles below, in a state of repair
legal recidivism, one who, after having been the subject of a conviction
irrevocable for a previous offense, commits another.
Article 155
Anyone who has been, by irrevocable decision, sentenced to
criminal sentence, has committed a second crime whatever its nature,
is condemned:
Forced residence for a period not exceeding ten years if the
penalty prescribed by law for the second crime is civic degradation;
Imprisonment of five to ten years, if the penalty prescribed by law for the
second crime is forced residence;
Imprisonment of ten to twenty years, if the penalty prescribed by law for the
second crime is imprisonment for five to ten years;

- 55 - Imprisonment of twenty to thirty years, if the maximum sentence
decreed by law for the second crime is imprisonment for twenty years;
To perpetual reclusion, if the maximum of the penalty decreed by the
law for the second crime is imprisonment for thirty years;
To the death penalty, if the first crime having been punished by imprisonment
life, the penalty prescribed by law for the second crime is the
perpetual reclusion on.
Article 156
Anyone who has been, by irrevocable decision, convicted of
crime with a penalty of more than one year of imprisonment, less than
five years after the expiration of this sentence or its prescription, committed a
crime or offense legally punishable by imprisonment,
must be sentenced to the maximum of this penalty, which may be higher
up to double.
The residence ban may, in addition, be imposed for a
duration of five to ten years.
Section 157
Anyone who has been, by irrevocable decision, convicted of an offense
to a prison sentence, has committed the same offense less than five
years after the expiration of this sentence or its prescription, must be
sentenced to a prison term which may not be less than
double that previously pronounced, without however being able to
exceed double the maximum penalty legally prescribed for the
new offense.
Article 158
Are considered to constitute the same offense for the
determination of recidivism, the offenses combined in one of the
paragraphs below:
1° Theft, fraud, breach of trust, abuse of authority, issuance
bad checks, forgery, use of forgery and bankruptcy
fraudulent, concealment of things resulting from a crime or misdemeanor;
2° Homicide by recklessness, injuries by recklessness, crime of
leak;

- 56 - 3° Indecent assault without violence, public outrage against modesty,
habitual excitement to debauchery, assistance in the prostitution of others;
4° Rebellion, violence and outrages against magistrates,
jury assessors, law enforcement officers;
5° All offenses committed by one spouse against the other
husband44;
6° All offenses committed against children under the age of ten -
eight Gregorian years45.
In the event that the law, to determine the penalty, refers to a
article of the penal code punishing another offense, the two offenses as well
assimilated from the point of view of the penalty, are considered for the
determination of recidivism as constituting the same offense.
Section 159
Anyone who has been convicted of a contravention has, within
twelve months from the delivery of this sentencing decision, which became
irrevocable, committed the same infraction, is punishable by the penalties
aggravated by repeat offenses in accordance with the
provisions of article 611.
Article 160
No one who has been convicted by a military tribunal is, in the event of
crime or misdemeanor committed subsequently, punishable by the penalties of recidivism,
as long as the conviction was pronounced by the military tribunal
for a crime or misdemeanor punishable under ordinary criminal laws.
SECTION V OF THE COMPETITION OF CAUSES OF ATTENUATION OR
AGGRAVATION
(Articles 161 and 162)
Section 161
In the event of a combination of causes of attenuation and aggravation, the
judge determines the sentence taking into account successively:

the offense;
Aggravating circumstances inherent to the personality of
the perpetrator of the offense;
Mitigating legal excuses inherent in the commission of
the offence;
Mitigating legal excuses inherent in the personality of
the perpetrator of the offense;
From the state of recidivism;
Extenuating circumstances.
Section 162
When the culprit is a minor and
the judge decides to apply
a penalty in execution of the provisions of article 517 of the code of
criminal procedure 46, the reduction or substitution of penalties provided for
said article are determined according to the sentence as it would have been
applicable to an adult offender by the effect of the provisions of article
previous.

- 58 - LLIIVVRREE IIIIII DDEESS DDIIVVEERRSSEESS IINNFFRRAACCTTIIOONNSS EETT DDEE
