(Articles 163 to 612)

TTIITTRREE PPRREEMMIIEERR DDEESS CCRRIIMMEESS,, DDEESS DDEELLIITTSS
CCOORRRREECCTTIIOONNNNEELLSS EETT DDEESS DDEELLIITTSS DDEE PPOOLLIICCEE
(Articles 163 to 607)

CCHHAAPPIITTRREE PPRREEMMIIEERR DDEESS CCRRIIMMEESS EETT DDEELLIITTSS CCOONNTTRREE LLAA
SAFETY DDEE LL’EETTAATT
(Articles 163 to 218)

SECTION I OF ATTACKS AND PLOTS AGAINST THE KING,
THE ROYAL FAMILY AND THE FORM OF GOVERNMENT
(Articles 163 to 180)

Article 163
An attack against the life or person of the King is punishable by death.
This attack is never excusable.
Article 164
The attack against the person of the King, when he did not have the
result of infringing on his freedom and that he did not cause him any outpouring of
blood, wounds or disease is punishable by life imprisonment.
Section 165
An attempt on the life of the Heir to the Throne is punishable by death.

- 59 - Article 166
The attack against the person of the Heir to the Throne is punishable by
perpetual reclusion.
When it has not resulted in an infringement of his freedom and
that he caused him neither bloodshed, nor wounds, nor illness, this
The attack is punishable by imprisonment for 20 to 30 years.
Article 167
Attempts against the lives of members of the royal family are punishable by
dead.
The attack against their person is punishable by imprisonment of 5 to 20 years.
When it has not resulted in an infringement of their freedom and
that he caused them neither bloodshed, nor wounds, nor illness, this
attack is punishable by 2 to 5 years of imprisonment.
Article 168
Are considered members of the royal family for
the application of the previous article: the ascendants of the King, his
direct lineal descendants, his wives, his brothers and their children of
two sexes, his sisters and his uncles.
Article 169
The attack whose aim is either to destroy or to change the Regime
or the order of succession to the Throne, or to take up arms
against royal authority is punishable by life imprisonment.
Section 170
The attack exists as soon as there is a punishable attempt.
Section 171
In the event that one of the crimes provided for in articles 163, 165, 167 and
169 was executed or simply attempted by a gang, the penalties enacted
to these articles are applied to all individuals, without distinction of
ranks, part of the gang and who were apprehended at the scene
of the seditious meeting.
The same sentences are pronounced against anyone who directed the
sedition, or exercised in the band any specific employment or

- 62 - command, even when he was not apprehended at the scene of the
meeting.
Article 172
Plotting against the life or person of the King is punishable by
perpetual reclusion, if it was followed by an act committed or begun
to prepare for its execution.
If it was not followed by any act committed or begun to
prepare for execution, the penalty is imprisonment for five to twenty years.
Article 173
The plot against the life of the Heir to the Throne is punished
in accordance with the previous article.
Plotting against the person of the Heir to the Throne is punishable by
imprisonment of ten to twenty years, if it was followed by an act committed or
started to prepare for its execution.
If it was not followed by any act committed or begun to
prepare for execution, the penalty is imprisonment for five to ten years.
Article 174
Conspiracy to achieve one of the ends mentioned in article 169 is
punished by imprisonment for ten to thirty years, if it was followed by an act committed
or started to prepare for its execution.
If it was not followed by any act committed or begun to
prepare for execution, the penalty is imprisonment for five to ten years.
Section 175
There is a conspiracy as soon as the resolution to act is concerted and decided
between two or more people.
Article 176
The proposal made and not approved to form a conspiracy against
life or the person of the King or the Heir to the Throne is punished with
imprisonment of five to ten years.

- 61 - Article 177
The proposal made and not accepted to form a conspiracy to
achieve one of the ends mentioned in article 169 is punishable by
imprisonment of two to five years.
Article 17 8
When an individual has formed the resolution alone
n to commit a
attack against the life or person of the King or against the life of the Heir
of the Throne and an act to prepare for its execution has been committed or
begun by him alone and without assistance, the punishment is that of seclusion
from five to ten years.
Item 17947
Is punishable by imprisonment of six months to two years and
fine of 20,000 to 200,000 dirhams or one of these two penalties
only anyone who defames, insults or offends
the person of the King or the person of the Heir to the Throne or a
violation of the respect due to the King.
Is punishable by imprisonment of three months to one year and
fine of 10,000 to 100,000 dirhams or one of these two penalties
only anyone who commits defamation, insult or offense against
the private lives of members of the royal family designated in article 168 of
this law.
The penalty referred to in two paragraphs above is doubled when the
defamation, insult or offense against the private life of the person of
King or towards the person of the Heir to the Throne or members of the
royal family or the violation of respect due to the King was committed either by
speeches, cries or threats uttered in public places or meetings or
by posters exposed to public view, or by sale,
distribution or by any means which meets the condition of advertising
including electronically, on paper and audiovisually.

47- The provisions of article 179 above have been repealed and replaced, in accordance
of article 2 of law no. 73 -15 modifying and supplementing certain provisions of the code
criminal law promulgated by Dahir No. 1 -16-104 of 13 Chaoual 1437 (July 18, 2016);
Official Bulletin No. 6522 of 1st Rabii I 1438 (December 1, 2016), p 1860.

- 62 - Article 180
In cases where, under one of the articles of this section,
only a criminal penalty is incurred, the culprits may be, in
in addition, struck for at least five years and twenty years at most
the prohibition of one or more of the rights mentioned in article 40 of the
this code;they may also be subject to a ban on
stay for a period of two to ten years.
SECTION II CRIMES AND OFFENSES AGAINST SECURITY
OUTSIDE THE STATE
(Articles 181 to 200)
Section 181
Is, in time of peace or in time of war, guilty of treason
and punished with death:
1° Any Moroccan who bears arms against Morocco;
2° Any Moroccan who maintains intelligence with an authority
foreign, with a view to inciting it to undertake hostilities against the
Morocco, or provides it with the means, either by facilitating the penetration of
foreign forces on Moroccan territory, or by undermining the loyalty
armies of land, sea or air, or in any other way;
3° Any Moroccan who delivers to a foreign authority or its agents,
either Moroccan troops, or territories, towns, fortresses,
works, posts, stores, arsenals, materials, munitions, vessels,
buildings or air navigation devices belonging to Morocco;
4° Any Moroccan who delivers to a foreign authority or its agents,
in whatever form and by whatever means, a secret of the
national defense or who ensures by any means whatsoever the
possession of a secret of this nature with a view to delivering it to an authority
foreign or its agents;
5° Any Moroccan who voluntarily destroys or damages a ship,
an air navigation device, equipment, supply,
construction or installation likely to be used for the
national defense or knowingly practices, either before or after their
completion, defects likely to prevent them from functioning, or
to cause an accident.

- 63 - Article 182
Is, in time of war, guilty of treason and punishable by death:
1° Any Moroccan who provokes soldiers or sailors to
pass into the service of a foreign authority, facilitates their means of doing so or
enlisted for an authority at war with Morocco;
2° Any Moroccan who maintains intelligence with an authority
foreign or with its agents with a view to favoring companies of this
authority against Morocco;
3° Any Moroccan who knowingly participates in a business of
demoralization of the army or the nation with the aim of harming the
national defense.
For the application of this article and that of article 181, are
assimilated to Moroccans, foreign soldiers or sailors in the service of
Morocco.
Section 183
Is, in time of peace, punishable by imprisonment of five to twenty years, any
Moroccan or foreigner who knowingly participates in a
enterprise of demoralization of the army with the aim of harming the
national defense.
Article 184
Is, in time of peace, punishable by imprisonment of five to thirty years, any
My
local or foreigner who is guilty of:
1° Willful faulty workmanship in the manufacture of war material,
when this defect is not likely to cause an accident;
2° Deterioration or intentional destruction of material or
supplies intended for or used for national defense;
3° Violent obstruction of the circulation of this material;
4° Voluntary participation in an action committed in a gang and in
open force, having as its aim and result one of the crimes foreseen
in the preceding paragraphs of this article, as well as the preparation
of said action.

- 64 - Article 185
Any foreigner who
commits any of the acts referred to in Article 181, paragraphs 2, 3, 4 and 5, and
section 182.
Section 186
Provocation to commit or offer to commit one of the crimes
referred to in articles 181 to 185 is punishable as the crime itself.
Article 187
Are deemed national defense secrets for the application of
this code:
1° Military, diplomatic and economic information
or industrial which, by their nature, should only be known to
persons qualified to hold them, and must, in the interest of
national defense, be kept secret from any other person;
2° Objects, materials, writings, drawings, plans, maps, surveys,
photographs or other reproductions, and all other documents
any which, by their nature, should only be known to
persons qualified to handle or hold them and must be required
secrets with regard to any other person as could lead to the
discovery of information belonging to one of the targeted categories
in the preceding paragraph;
3° Military information of all kinds, not provided
public by the Government and not included in the lists
above, including publication, broadcast, disclosure or
reproduction will have been prohibited by a dahir or by a decree in council
office;
4° Information relating to either the measures taken to
discover and arrest the perpetrators and accomplices of crimes or offenses against
the external security of the State, or in the course of prosecutions and
the investigation, or the debates before the trial court.
Article 188
The following are guilty of endangering the external security of the State:
1° Any Moroccan or foreigner who, through hostile acts
approved by the Government, exposes Morocco to a declaration of

- 65 - war;

2° Any Moroccan or foreigner who, through acts not approved by
the Government, exposes Moroccans to suffering reprisals.
When the offenses provided for in paragraphs 1 and 2 are
committed in time of war, they are punishable by imprisonment of five to
thirty years.
When committed in peacetime, they are punished with
imprisonment of one to five years and a fine of 1,000 to 10,000
dirhams.
Section 189
Is guilty of endangering the external security of the State and punishable by
imprisonment of five to thirty years:
1° Any Moroccan or foreigner who, in time of war, maintains
without authorization from the Government, correspondence or
relations with the subjects of a power or the agents of an authority
enemy;
2° Any Moroccan or foreigner who, in time of war, in contempt
prohibitions enacted, performs acts directly or through
of commerce with the subjects of a power or the agents of an authority
enemy.
Article 190
Every Moroccan is guilty of undermining the external security of the State.
or foreigner who has undertaken, by whatever means, to carry
attack on the integrity of Moroccan territory.
When the offense was committed during wartime, the offender
is punished by death.
When it was committed in peacetime, the culprit is punished with
imprisonment of five to twenty years.
Article 191
Anyone who is guilty of endangering the external security of the State
maintains with the agents of a foreign authority intelligence having
for the purpose or having the effect of harming the military situation or
diplomatic of Morocco.

- 66 - When the offense was committed in time of war, the penalty is
that of imprisonment of five to thirty years.
When it was committed in peacetime, the penalty is that of
imprisonment of one to five years and a fine of 1,000 to 10,000
dirhams.
Section 192
The following are guilty of endangering the external security of the State:
1° Any Moroccan or foreigner who, for a purpose other than that of
deliver to a foreign authority or its agents, ensures, by some means
whatever means, the possession of a national defense secret or the
carries, in any form and by any means, to the
knowledge of the public or an unqualified person;
2° Any Moroccan or foreigner who, through imprudence, negligence or
non-observance of rules
regulations, allows it to be destroyed, subtracted or removed,
all or in part, and even momentarily, objects, materials,
documents or information entrusted to him, and whose
knowledge could lead to discovery of a defense secret
national, or lets take, even in part, knowledge, copy or
reproduction;
3° Any Moroccan or foreigner who, without prior authorization from
the competent authority, delivers or communicates to a person acting
on behalf of a foreign authority or company, either a
invention of interest to national defense, i.e. information,
studies or manufacturing processes relating to an invention of this
gender, or to an industrial application of interest to national defense.
When the offenses provided for in the preceding paragraphs are
committed in time of war, the penalty is imprisonment for five to
thirty years.
When committed in peacetime, the penalty is that of
imprisonment of one to five years and a fine of 1,000 to 10,000
dirhams.
Section 193
The following are guilty of endangering the external security of the State:
1° Any Moroccan or foreigner who enters in disguise
or a false name, or by concealing his status or nationality, in a

- 67 - fortress, a work, post or arsenal, in works, camps,
bivouacs or cantonments of an army, in a warship,
or a commercial vessel used for national defense, in
an aerial navigation device or in a military vehicle, in
a military or maritime establishment of any kind or in a
establishment or construction site working for national defense;
2° Any Moroccan or foreigner who, even without disguising themselves, or without
conceal his name, his status or his nationality, has organized a
occult manner, any means of correspondence or
remote transmission likely to harm national defense;
3° Any Moroccan or foreigner who flies over Moroccan territory
by means of a foreign aircraft without being authorized to do so by a convention
diplomatic or permission from the Moroccan authority;
4° Any Moroccan or foreigner who, in a fixed prohibition zone
by the military or maritime authority, carried out without the latter's authorization,
drawings, photographs, surveys or topographical operations
inside or around places, structures, posts or establishments
military and maritime;
5° Any Moroccan or foreigner who stays, in defiance of a
prohibition decreed by legitimate authority, within a specified radius
around fortified works or military establishments and
maritime.
When the offenses provided for in the preceding paragraphs are
committed in time of war, the penalty is imprisonment for five to
thirty years.
When committed in peacetime, the penalty is that of
imprisonment of one to five years and a fine of 1,000 to 10,000
dirhams.
Section 194
Is guilty of endangering the external security of the State and punished by
imprisonment of one to five years and a fine of 1,000 to 10,000
dirhams any Moroccan or foreigner who, in time of war, has completed
knowingly an act likely to harm national defense, other than
those listed in previous articles.

- 68 - Article 195
Is guilty of endangering the external security of the State and punished by
imprisonment of one to five years and a fine of 1,000 to 10,000
dirhams any Moroccan or foreigner who, in times of peace, enlists
soldiers in Moroccan territory on behalf of a foreign authority.
The same penalty is applicable to the author of this offense in time of
war, unless the act constitutes a more serious offense.
Section 196
Independently of the application of article 129 repressing the
complicity and article 571 punishing concealment, is punished as an accomplice
or as a receiver:
1° Any Moroccan or foreigner who, knowing the intentions of
perpetrators of crimes or misdemeanors, against the external security of the State, their
provides subsidies, means of livelihood, housing, place of retirement or
meeting; meeting;
2° Any Moroccan or foreigner who knowingly carries the
correspondence of the perpetrators of a crime or offense against security
outside the State or knowingly facilitates them in any way
either the search, concealment, transport or transmission of the object of the
crime or misdemeanor;
3° Any Moroccan or foreigner who knowingly conceals objects or
instruments having been used or intended to be used to commit the said crimes or
crimes or the objects, materials or documents obtained by these crimes or
crimes;
4° Any Moroccan or foreigner who knowingly destroys, subtracts,
conceals, conceals or alters a public or private document which was
nature to facilitate the search for the crime or offense provided for in the
preceding paragraphs, the discovery of evidence, or the punishment of
its authors.
However, the
trial court may exempt from the penalty
incurred by the persons designated in this article who have not
otherwise participated in the crime or misdemeanor, when they are
relatives or allies of the perpetrator of the offense, up to the fourth degree
inclusively.

- 69 - Article 197
In cases where, under one of the articles of this section
only a criminal penalty is incurred, this penalty can be imposed
up to double with regard to the offenses referred to in articles 188, paragraph 1,
191 and 193. The guilty can, in addition, be punished for five years
at least and at most twenty years of the ban on one or more of the
rights mentioned in article 40 of this code;they can also
be subject to a residence ban for a period of two to ten years.
Section 198
Moroccan law applies to crimes and offenses against security
external force of the State committed inside or outside the territory of the
Kingdom.
The prosecution of offenses committed abroad is not
subject to the conditions provided for by articles 751 to 756 of the code of
criminal procedure48.
The attempted offense is punished as the completed offense.
Article 199
Confiscation of the object of the crime or offense and the objects and
instruments used to commit it must be obligatorily
pronounced without there being any reason to inquire whether or not they belong
to the condemned.
The remuneration received by the culprit, or the amount of its value
when the remuneration could not be seized, must be declared acquired at the
Treasure by judgment.
When the attack on the external security of the State was committed in
time of war, the culprit may be sentenced to confiscation of a
part of his property not exceeding half.
Section 200
The provisions of this section do not prevent
the application, in the cases provided for by them, of the provisions enacted
by the codes of military justice for the army and for the army of
sea in matters of treason and espionage.

48 - Articles 707 to 712 of Law No. 22.01 relating to the aforementioned criminal procedure.

- 72 - SECTION III CRIMES AND OFFENSES AGAINST SECURITY
INTERIOR OF THE STATE
(Articles 201 to 207)
Article 201
Is guilty of endangering the internal security of the State and punishable by
dead, any perpetrator of an attack whose aim is to provoke war
civil society by arming or inciting residents to arm themselves against each other
others, either to bring devastation, massacre and pillage in one or
several douars or localities.
A conspiracy formed for the same purpose is punishable by imprisonment for five
at twenty years if it was followed by an act committed or started to
prepare for execution.
If the conspiracy was not followed by any act committed or begun for
prepare the execution, the penalty is that of imprisonment of one to
five years.
The proposal made and not approved to form the conspiracy is punished
imprisonment of six months to three years.
Section 202
Is guilty of endangering the internal security of the State and punishable by
death:
1° Any person who, without right or legitimate reason, takes or exercises
command of an army unit, one or more buildings
of war, one or more military aircraft, a stronghold, a
military post, port or town;
2° Any person who keeps, against the order of the Government, a
any military command;
3° Any commander who maintains his army or his troop
assembled after dismissal or separation has been ordered;
4° Any person who, without order or authorization from the authorities
legitimate, raises or causes to be raised armed troops, engages or enlists, makes
engage or enlist soldiers or supply or procure weapons or
ammunition.

- 71 - Article 203
Is guilty of endangering the internal security of the State and punishable by
dead, any person who, either to seize public funds, or
to invade domains, properties, places, towns, fortresses, posts,
stores, arsenals, ports, vessels or buildings, belonging to the State,
either to plunder or share national public properties, or those
of a generality of citizens, either finally to attack or resist
towards the public force acting against the perpetrators of these crimes,
put at the head of armed bands, or exercised a function there or
command of any kind.
The same penalty is applied to those who led the association, raised
or raised, organized or caused seditious bands to be organized or have,
knowingly and voluntarily supplied or procured weapons, ammunition and
instruments of crime, or sent food convoys, or who have
otherwise provided assistance to leaders or commanders
bands.
Section 204
In the event that one of the crimes provided for in
article 201 has been executed or
simply tempted by a gang, the penalties laid down in this article are,
under the conditions provided for in article 171, applied to all individuals
without distinction of ranks being part of the band.
Section 205
In the event that the seditious meeting had as its object or result one
of the crimes provided for in article 203 the individuals belonging to these gangs
without exercising any command or specific employment and who
would have been apprehended at the scene of the meeting are punished with
imprisonment of five to twenty years.
Section 206
Is guilty of endangering the internal security of the State and punishable by
imprisonment of one to five years and a fine of 1,000 to 10,000
dirhams whoever, directly or indirectly, receives from a person
or a foreign organization and in any form whatsoever,
donations, presents, loans or other advantages intended or used in any
or in part to carry out or remunerate in Morocco an activity or a
propaganda likely to undermine the integrity, sovereignty, or

- 72 - to the independence of the Kingdom, or to shake the loyalty that the citizens
owe to the State and the institutions of the Moroccan people.
Section 207
In the cases provided for in the preceding article, the confiscation of funds
or objects received must be pronounced.
The culprit may, in addition, be banned, in whole or in part, from
rights mentioned in article 40.
SECTION IV PROVISIONS COMMON TO THIS CHAPTER
(Articles 208 to 218)
Section 208
Those who, knowing the purpose and character of armed bands
provided for in articles 171, 203 and 205, have, without constraint, provided them with
accommodation, places of retirement or meeting, are punishable by imprisonment of
five to ten years.
Section 209
Is guilty of failure to disclose an attack against state security and
punishable by imprisonment of two to five years and a fine of 1,000 to
10,000 dirhams any person who, having knowledge of projects or
acts tending to commit acts punishable by a criminal penalty by
the provisions of this chapter, does not do so, from the moment it
knew them, the declaration to the judicial, administrative or
military.
Article 210
In the case provided for in the preceding article, the culprit may, in addition,
be subject to the prohibition of one or more of the rights mentioned in
Article 40 and a ban on stay which may not exceed ten years.
Article 211
Benefits from an absolute excuse, under the conditions provided for in the
articles 143 to 145, that of the culprits who, before any execution or
attempt to commit a crime or misdemeanor against the security of the State, was the first

- 73 - given to the authorities referred to in Article 209 knowledge of these offenses
and their perpetrators or accomplices.
Section 212
The absolutory excuse provided for in the preceding article is only
optional if the denunciation occurs after consumption or
attempted crime or misdemeanor, but before the initiation of proceedings.
Section 213
Benefit from an absolute excuse for acts of sedition
provided for in sections 203 to 205, those who, having been part of gangs
armies without exercising any command and without fulfilling any
determined employment, withdrew at the first warning from the authorities
civil or military or even later when they were
apprehended outside the scene of the seditious meeting, without weapons and without
put up resistance.
Article 214
Beneficiaries of absolutory excuse remain punishable with reason
other crimes or offenses that they have personally committed
course or on the occasion of sedition.
Section 215
Individuals who have been exempted from punishment by application of the
two articles 211 and 213 may, by virtue of the provisions of article
145, be subject to security measures.
Section 216
The crimes and offenses provided for in this chapter are investigated and
judged by priority, as urgent matters.
Section 217
The decision to refer the indictment chamber to the court
criminal cannot, in the matters provided for in this chapter, make
the subject of the appeal in cassation of article 451 (last paragraph) of

- 74 - code of criminal procedure e49, excluding the special appeal referred to in
article 452 of the same code50.
Section 218
For the execution of sentences, crimes and offenses provided for herein
chapter are considered as common law crimes and misdemeanors.

Article 218 -1
Constitute acts of terrorism, when they are
intentionally in connection with a sole proprietorship or
collective whose aim is the serious attack on public order by
intimidation, terror or violence, the following offenses:
1) intentional harm to people's lives or their integrity, or
to

2) counterfeiting or falsification of currencies or credit instruments
public, state seals and hallmarks, stamps and marks, or the
forgery or falsification referred to in articles 360, 361 and 362 hereof
code;
3) destruction, damage or deterioration;
4) the hijacking, damage of aircraft or ships or
any other means of transport, degradation of transport facilities
air, sea and land navigation and the destruction,
degradation or deterioration of means of communication;
5) theft and extortion of property;
6) the manufacture, possession, transport, putting into circulation or
the illegal use of weapons, explosives or munitions;

Section 316
Is punishable by imprisonment of one to five years and a fine of 2,000 to 10,000 dirhams
without this fine being less than twenty-five percent of the amount of the check or
insufficient provision:
1) the drawer of a check who fails to maintain or provide funds for the check in view
from payment to presentation;
2) the drawer of the check who irregularly forbids the drawee from paying;
3) any person who forges or falsifies a check;
4) any person who, knowingly, agrees to receive, endorse or endorse
a falsified or counterfeit check;
5) any person who, knowingly, uses or attempts to use a check
counterfeit or falsified;
6) any person who, knowingly, agrees to receive or endorse a check
provided that it is not cashed immediately and that it is kept as
guaranteed.
Counterfeit or falsified checks will be confiscated and destroyed.Confiscation of materials,

of said checks will be pronounced by court decision, except when they have been used without knowledge
of the owner.

subject of this title:
1) those who have counterfeited or falsified a means of payment;
2) those who, knowingly, have used or attempted to use a means of
payment, counterfeit or falsified;
3) those who, knowingly, have agreed to receive payment by any means
payment, counterfeit or falsified.

- 76 - Article 218 -1-153
The following acts constitute terrorism offenses:
- the act of rallying or attempting to rally individually or
collectively, in an organized or unorganized framework, to entities,
organizations, bands or groups, terrorists, whatever their
form, their purpose, or the place where they are located, even if the
terrorist acts are not intended to harm the Kingdom of
Morocco or its interests;
- the fact of receiving or attempting to receive training or
training whatever the form, nature or duration
inside or outside the Kingdom of Morocco, with a view to
commit an act of terrorism inside or outside the
Kingdom regardless of the occurrence of such an act;
- the fact of enlisting by any means whatsoever, training or
train or attempt to enlist, train or train one or more
several people, with a view to joining entities,
organizations, bands or groups, terrorists within or outside
the outside of you
rrorism of the Kingdom of Morocco.
The aforementioned acts are punishable by imprisonment for five to ten years and
a fine of 5,000 to 10,000 dirhams.
The sanctions provided for in the preceding paragraph are increased to double
when it comes to enlisting, training or training a minor or when,
to do this, the supervision of schools, institutes or centers
education or training, of any nature whatsoever, has been
exploited.
However, when the author of the offense is a legal entity,
he is punished with a fine of 1,000,000 to 10,000,000 dirhams in
pronouncing against it the dissolution as well as security measures
provided for in article 62 of this code, subject to the rights of third parties and

Article 218 -254
Is punishable by imprisonment of 2 to 6 years and a fine of
10,000 to 200,000 dirhams, anyone who advocates acts constituting
terrorism offenses, through speeches, cries or threats made
in public places or meetings or by writing, printed matter
sold, distributed or offered for sale or displayed in places or meetings
public either by posters exposed to public view by
different means of audio-visual and electronic information.
Is punished with the same penalty, anyone who, by any of the means
provided for in the first paragraph of this article, propaganda, apology or
the promotion of a person, entity, organization, band or group
terrorists.
However, when the perpetrator of the offense is a legal entity,
he is punished with a fine of 1,000,000 to 10,000,000 dirhams in
pronouncing against it the dissolution as well as the security measures
provided for in article 62 of this code, subject to the rights of third parties and
without prejudice to the sanctions which could be pronounced against
of its directors or agents having committed or attempted to commit
the offense.
Article 218 -3
Also constitutes an act of terrorism, within the meaning of the first
paragraph of article 218 -1 above, the fact of introducing or putting into
the atmosphere, on the ground, in the subsoil or in water, including
those of the territorial sea, a substance which endangers the health of
man or animals or the natural environment.
The acts provided for in the first paragraph above are punishable by ten to
twenty years of imprisonment.

- 78 - The penalty is life imprisonment, when the facts resulted in
mutilation, amputation or deprivation of the use of a limb, blindness,
loss of an eye or any other permanent disability for one or
several people.
The culprit is punished with death when the facts resulted in death
of one or more people.
Article 218 -455
The following offenses constitute acts of terrorism:
- the fact of providing, gathering or managing by any means
either, directly or indirectly, funds, values or property
with the intention of seeing them used r or knowing that they will be used, in
in whole or in part, with a view to committing an act of terrorism,
regardless of the occurrence of such an act;
- providing assistance or giving advice for this purpose.
The offenses referred to in this article are punishable:
* for individuals, from five to twenty years of imprisonment and
a fine of 500,000 to 2,000,000 dirhams;
* for legal entities, a fine of 1,000,000 to 5,000,000
of dirhams, without prejudice to the penalties which could be pronounced
against their directors or agents involved in the offenses.
The penalty is increased to ten years and thirty years of imprisonment and the fine
double:
- when the offenses are committed using the facilities that
provides the exercise of a professional activity;
- when the offenses are committed by an organized gang;
- in the event of a recurrence.
The person guilty of financing terrorism is liable, in
in addition, the confiscation of all or part of his property.

- 79 - Article 218-4-156
In the event of conviction for an offense of financing the
terrorism or for a terrorism offense, total confiscation
things, objects and goods which were used or were to be used in the offense
or which are the product or equivalent value of the said things
objects, goods or product must be pronounced, subject to the rights of
third party in good faith.
Article 218 -4-257
For the application of the provisions of articles 218 -4 and 218 -4-1 of the
this law, we mean by:
- Products: all goods coming, directly or indirectly, from
one of the offenses provided for in the aforementioned articles;
- Assets: all types of tangible or intangible assets, movable or
buildings, divided or undivided, as well as acts or documents
legal, whatever their medium, including in the form
electronic or digital, attesting the ownership of these assets or
rights attached to it.
Article 218 -558
Whoever, by any means whatsoever, persuades, incites or
provokes another to commit one of the offenses provided for herein
chapter, is punishable by imprisonment of five to ten years and a fine of
5,000 to 10,000 dirhams.
The sanctions provided for in the preceding paragraph are increased to double
when it comes to persuading, inciting or provoking a minor or
when, to do so, the supervision of schools, institutes or centers
education or training, of any nature whatsoever, has been
exploited.
However, when the perpetrator of the offense is a legal entity,
he is punished with a fine of 1,000,000 to 10,000,000 dirhams in
pronouncing against it the dissolution as well as security measures

Article 218 -6
In addition to the cases of complicity provided for in article 129 of this code,
is punishable by imprisonment for ten to twenty years, anyone who knowingly provides
to a person who is the author, co-perpetrator or accomplice of a terrorist act, i.e.
weapons, ammunition or instruments of the offense, or contributions
pecuniary, means of subsistence, correspondence or
transportation, or a place of meeting, accommodation or retirement or which
helps to dispose of the proceeds of their misdeeds, or who, from any other
manner, knowingly assists them.
However, the court may exempt from the penalty incurred
relatives or relatives up to the fourth degree, inclusive, of the author,
of the co-perpetrator or accomplice of a terrorist act, when they have only
provided to the latter accommodation or personal means of subsistence.
Article 218 -7
The maximum penalties provided for the offenses referred to in
article 218 -1 above, is noted as follows, when the acts committed
constitute terrorism offences:
- death when the penalty provided for is life imprisonment;
- perpetual reclusion when the maximum penalty provided for is
30 years of imprisonment;
- the maximum custodial sentences are increased to double,
without exceeding thirty years when the penalty provided for is imprisonment or
imprisonment;
- when the penalty provided for is a fine, the maximum penalty
is multiplied by one hundred without being less than 100,000 dirhams;
- when the author is a legal entity, the dissolution of the
legal entity as well as the two security measures provided for in article
62 of the penal code must be pronounced subject to the rights
of others.

- 81 - Article 218 -8
Is guilty of non-disclosure of terrorism offenses and punished
imprisonment of five to ten years, any person who, having knowledge
plans or acts tending to commit acts constituting
terrorism offenses, does not do any, from the moment she has them
known, the declaration to the judicial and security authorities,
administrative or military.
However, the court may, in the case provided for in the first paragraph of
this article, exempt from the penalty incurred parents or allies
up to the fourth degree, inclusive, of the author,
of the co-author or
accessory to a terrorism offense.
When it comes to a legal entity, the penalty is a fine of
100,000 to 1,000,000 dirhams.
Article 218 -9
Benefits from an absolute excuse, under the conditions provided for in the
articles 143 to 145 of this code, the author, co-author or accomplice
who, before any attempt to commit a terrorism offense
being the subject of an agreement or association and before any implementation
public action movement, was the first to reveal to the authorities
judicial, security, administrative or military agreement established or
the existence of the association.
When the denunciation took place after the offense, the penalty is
reduced by half for the author, co-author or accomplice who
present ex officio to the authorities mentioned above or who denounces the
co-perpetrators or accomplices in the offense.
When the penalty provided for is death, it is commuted to the penalty of
reclusion perpetua, when it comes to the penalty of reclusion
perpetual, it is commuted to imprisonment of 20 to 30 years.

Whoever, by violence or threats, has forced or

- 84 - SECTION III ABUSE OF AUTHORITY COMMITTED BY
OPERATING AGAINST INDIVIDUALS AND PRACTICE
TORTURE64
(Articles 224 to 232)
A
article 224
Are deemed public officials, for the application of the law
criminal, all persons who, under a name and to an extent
any, are invested with a function or mandate even
temporary, paid or free and contribute as such, to the service of
the State, public administrations, municipalities,
public establishments or a service of public interest.
The status of public official is assessed on the day of the offense;
however, it persists after the cessation of functions when it has facilitated
or permitted the commission of the offense.
Section 225
Any magistrate, any public official, any agent or employee of
the authority or public force which orders or performs any act
arbitrary, infringing either on individual freedom or on the rights
civic rights of one or more citizens, is punishable by civic degradation.
If he justifies having acted by order of his hierarchical superiors in
an area of their competence, for which he owed them obedience, he
benefits from an absolute pardon.In this case, the penalty is applied
only to superiors who gave the order.
If the arbitrary act or act detrimental to individual freedom was
committed or ordered in private interest or for the satisfaction of
personal passions, the penalty incurred is that laid down in articles 436
at 440.

64 - Title of section II of chapter II of title one of book III of the completed penal code
by Article 1 of Law No. 43-04 amending and supplementing the Penal Code promulgated by
dahir n° 1 -06-20 of 15 moharrem 1427 (February 14, 2006), Official Bulletin n° 5400 of 1
safar 1427 (March 2, 2006), p.342.

- 85 - Article 226
The crimes provided for in article 225 give rise to civil liability
personal of their author as well as that of the State, unless appealed by this
last against the said author.
Section 227
Public officials, law enforcement officers,
employees of the public authority, responsible for the administrative police or
judicial, who have refused or neglected to respond to a complaint tending
to establish illegal and arbitrary detention, either in the
establishments or premises assigned to the custody of detainees, either everywhere
elsewhere, and who do not justify having reported it to the authority
superior, are punished with civic degradation.
Section 228
Any supervisor or guard of a penitentiary establishment or a
premises assigned to the custody of detainees which received a prisoner without one of the
regular detention titles provided for in article 653 of the procedural code
criminal65 or refused, without justifying the defense of the investigating magistrate,
to present this prisoner to the authorities or persons authorized to do so
visit, under the provisions of articles 660 to 662 of the code of
criminal proceedings66, or refused to present his records to the said
authorized persons, is guilty of arbitrary detention and punished with
imprisonment of six months to two years and a fine of 20,067 to 500
dirhams.
Section 229
Any magistrate of the judicial order, any judicial police officer
who, except in the case of flagrante delicto, provokes prosecution, renders or signs
an order or judgment, or issues a court warrant to
against a person who was the beneficiary of immunity, without
having previously obtained the release of this immunity in the
legal forms, is punished with civic degradation.

- 86 - Article 230
Any magistrate, any public official, any agent or employee of
the authority or public force which, acting as such, introduces itself
in the home of an individual, against the will of the latter, except in cases
provided for by law, is punishable by imprisonment of one month to one year and
a fine of 20,068 to 500 dirhams.
The provisions of article 225, paragraph 2°, are applicable to
the offense provided for in this article.
Item 23169
Any magistrate, any public official, any agent or employee of
the authority or public force which, without legitimate reason, uses or causes to be used
violence against people in the exercise or on the occasion of
the exercise of his functions, is punished for this violence and according to their
severity, following the provisions of articles 401 to 403;but the pain
applicable is aggravated as follows:
If it is a police offense or a criminal offense, the penalty
applicable is increased to twice that provided for the offense;
If it is a crime punishable by imprisonment for five to ten years, the penalty
is imprisonment of ten to fifteen years
;
If it is a crime punishable by imprisonment for ten to twenty years, the penalty
is imprisonment for twenty to thirty years.
Article 231 –170
For the purposes of this section, the term torture means any act which
causes acute physical or mental pain or suffering,
committed intentionally by or at the hands of a public official
instigation or with its express or tacit consent, inflicted on a
person for the purpose of intimidating or putting pressure on them or making
pressure on a third person, to obtain information or
indications or confessions, to punish her for an act that she or someone
third party has committed or is suspected of having committed or

68 - Ibid.
69 - Article modified and supplemented by article 2 of law no. 43-04, cited above.
66 - Articles added by article 3 of law no. 43-04, cited above.

- 87 - when such pain or suffering is inflicted for any other reason
based on any form of discrimination.
This term does not extend to pain or suffering resulting
only legal sanctions or caused by these sanctions or
which are inherent to them.
Article 231 -2
Without prejudice to more serious penalties, is punishable by imprisonment of five to
fifteen years and a fine of 10,000 to 30,000 dirhams
public official who practiced the torture provided for in article 231 -1 below
on it.
Article 231 -3
Without prejudice to more serious penalties, the penalty is imprisonment for ten to
twenty years and a fine of 20,000 to 50,000 dirhams if the torture is
committed:
- on a magistrate, a public force agent or a civil servant
public in the exercise or during the exercise of its functions;
- on a witness, a victim or a civil party either because he made a
deposition, filed a complaint or initiated legal action either for
prevent him from making a statement, filing a complaint or initiating a
legal action;
- by several people acting as perpetrators or accomplices;
- with premeditation or with use or threat of a weapon.
Article 231 -4
The penalty is life imprisonment when torture is committed on
a minor under 18 years old;
- when committed against a person in a vulnerable situation,
due to age, illness, disability, physical deficiency
or psychological is apparent or known to the author of the torture;
- when committed on a pregnant woman whose pregnancy is
apparent or known to the perpetrator of the torture;
- when it is preceded, accompanied or followed by sexual assault.
- The same penalty is applicable when torture is carried out in a manner
usual.


- 88 - Article 231 –5
Without prejudice to more serious penalties, when torture results in
mutilation, amputation, deprivation of use of a limb, blindness, loss
of one eye or any other permanent infirmity the penalty is imprisonment
from ten to twenty years.
In the event of premeditation or use of a weapon, the penalty is imprisonment for
twenty to thirty years.
Article 231 –6
Without prejudice to more serious penalties, any torture which results in death
without intention of giving it is punishable by imprisonment of twenty to thirty
years.
In case of premeditation or use of weapons, the penalty is imprisonment.
perpetual.
Article 231 -7
In all cases provided for in articles 231 -2 to 231 -6, the court must,
when it pronounces a criminal sentence, order the prohibition of
the exercise of one or more of the civil, civil or family rights referred to
in article 26 of this code for a period of two to ten years.
Article 231 -8
In all cases provided for in articles 231 -2 to 231 -6 above, the
court must, in pronouncing the conviction, order:
- confiscation of things and objects used to commit torture;
- the publication and display of its decision in accordance with the
provisions of article 48 of this code.
Article 23 2
Any public official, any Government agent, any
employee or employee of the postal service who opens, diverts or
deletes letters entrusted to the post office or which facilitates their opening, the
diversion or deletion71, is punishable by imprisonment of
three months to five years and a fine of 20,072 to 1,000 dirhams.

(Articles 233 to 262)
SECTION I OF THE COALITION OF OFFICIALS
(Articles 233 to 236)
Section 233
When measures contrary to the laws have been concerted, either by
a meeting of individuals or bodies depository of some part of
public authority, either by deputation or correspondence, the
guilty are punished with imprisonment of one month to six months.
They may, in addition, be subject to a ban on one or more
of the rights mentioned in article 40, and to exercise any function or employment
public for up to ten years.
Section 234
When measures against the execution of laws or orders of the
Government were concerted by one of the means set out in article
precedent, the guilty are punished with forced residence for a
duration not exceeding ten years.
When these measures have been agreed between the civil authorities and
the military bodies or their leaders, those who provoked them are punished
imprisonment of five to ten years, the other culprits are punished with
forced residence for a period not exceeding ten years.
Section 235
In the event that concerted measures between civil authorities and
the military bodies or their leaders, had as their object or result

- 92 - to attack the internal security of the State, the provocateurs are punished by
death and the others guilty of perpetual reclusion.
Section 236
All magistrates and public officials who have, by deliberation,
stopped to resign in order to prevent or
suspend either the administration of justice or the functioning of a
public service, are punished with civic degradation.
SECTION II ENCROACHMENT OF AUTHORITIES
ADMINISTRATIVE AND JUDICIAL AND DENIAL OF JUSTICE
(Articles 237 to 240)
Section 237
Are punished with civic degradation, all magistrates or officers of
police which:
1° Have interfered in the exercise of legislative power, either by
enacting regulations containing legislative provisions, either in
stopping or suspending the execution of one or more laws;
2° Interfered in matters attributed to the authorities
administrative, either by issuing regulations on these matters, or by
forbidding him to carry out the orders of the administration.
Section 238
All governors, pashas, super bosses, bosses or others
administrators who interfere, either in the exercise of legislative power
by issuing regulations containing legislative provisions, or by
stopping or suspending the execution of one or more laws, either in
the exercise of judicial power by issuing orders or defenses to
courts or tribunals, are punished with civic degradation.
Article 239
All governors, pashas, super bosses, bosses or others
directors who, except in cases provided for by law and despite the
protest of the parties or one of them, ruled on matters of
the jurisdiction of the courts or tribunals, are punishable by imprisonment
from one month to two years and a fine of 50 to 500 dirhams.

- 91 - Article 240
Any magistrate or any public official vested with powers
jurisdictional authorities which, under any pretext whatsoever, even silence
or the obscurity of the law, has denied doing the justice he owes to
parties after having been requested to do so and who persevered in his denial, after
warning or injunction from his superiors, can be prosecuted and
punished with a fine of at least 250 dirhams and not more than 2,500 dirhams
and the ban on the exercise of public functions for a period
from one to ten years.

- 92 - SECTION III DIVERSIONS AND CONCUSSIONS
COMMITTED BY PUBLIC OFFICIALS73
(Articles 241 to 247)
Item 24174
Any judge, any public official who misappropriates, dissipates,
unduly withholds or subtracts public or private funds, securities in
in lieu or documents, titles, deeds, movable effects which were between
his hands, either by virtue or because of his functions, is punished with
imprisonment of five years to twenty years and a fine of 5,000 to 100,000
dirhams.
If things diverted, dissipated, withheld or subtracted are
of a value less than 100,000 dirhams, the culprit is punished with
imprisonment of two years to five years and a fine of 2,000 to
50,000 dirhams.

Any holder of

the State;the beneficiary is punished as an accomplice.

- 95 - SECTION IV CORRUPTION AND TRAFFICKING IN INFLUENCE78
(Articles 248 to 256)
Item 24879
Is guilty of corruption and punished with imprisonment of two to
five years and a fine of 2,000 to 50,000 dirhams whoever requests
or accepts offers or promises, solicits or receives donations, presents
or other advantages, for:
1° Being a magistrate, public official or being invested with a mandate
elective, perform or refrain from performing an act of one's function, just
or not, but not subject to remuneration or an act which, although outside
of his personal attributions, is, or could have been, facilitated by his function;
2° Being an arbitrator or expert appointed either by the administrative authority
or judicial, either by the parties, render a decision or give a
favorable or unfavorable opinion;
3° Being a magistrate, jury assessor or member of a court,
decide either in favor or to the detriment of a party;
4° Being a doctor, surgeon, dentist, midwife, certify
falsely or conceal the existence of illnesses or infirmities or a
state of pregnancy or providing misleading information on the origin
of illness or infirmity or the cause of death.
When the sum is greater than 100,000 dirhams, the penalty is
five to ten years of imprisonment and a fine of 5,000 to 100,000 dirhams.
Item 24980
Is guilty of corruption and punished with imprisonment of one to
three years and a fine of 5,000 to 50,000 dirhams, all committed,
salaried or remunerated employee or employee in any form,

consent of his boss, is requested or approved of the offers or
promises, is solicited or received donations, presents, commissions,
discounts or premiums for doing or refraining from doing an act of

- 98 - SECTION V ABUSE OF AUTHORITY COMMITTED BY
OFFICIALS AGAINST PUBLIC ORDER
(Articles 257 to 260)
Section 257
Any magistrate or public official who requires or orders, makes
request or order the action or use of public force against
the execution of a law or against the collection of a contribution
legally established or against the execution of either an order or
judicial mandate, or any other order emanating from legitimate authority,
is punishable by imprisonment of one to five years.
The culprit may, in addition, be punished for at least five years and
ten years at most from the prohibition of one or more of the rights mentioned
in section 40;he may also be banned from exercising
any public functions or employment for a maximum of ten years.
Section 258
When the magistrate or public official justifies having acted by
order of his hierarchical superiors in an area of their
competence, for which he owed them obedience, he benefits from a
absolute excuse.In this case, the penalty is applied only to
superiors who gave the order.
Article 259
If the orders or requisitions were the direct cause of a qualified fact
crime by law, the penalty for this crime is applicable to the culprit
abuse of authority.
Section 260
Any commander, officer or non-commissioned officer of the public force who,
after having been legally requested by the civil authority, refused or
abstained from causing the force placed under his orders to act, is punished by
imprisonment of one to six months.
Section VI The exercise of public authority illegally anticipated or
extended

- 99 - (Articles 261 and 262)
Section 261
Any magistrate or public official bound by an oath
professional who, except in cases of necessity, begins to exercise his
functions without having taken the oath, is punishable by a fine of 20085 to 500
dirhams.
Section 262
Every magistrate, every public official dismissed, killed,
suspended or legally prohibited who, after receiving official notice from the
decision concerning him, continues the exercise of his functions, is punished by
imprisonment of six months to two years and a fine of 200 to 1,000
dirhams.
Any elective public official or
temporary worker who continues to exercise his functions after their cessation
legal.
The culprit may also be banned from practicing
any public functions or employment for a maximum of ten years.

SECTION I OUTRAGE AND VIOLENCE AGAINST PU OFFICIALS
BL IC
(Articles 263 to 267)
Article 263
Is punishable by imprisonment of one month to one year and a fine
from 250 to 5,000 dirhams, anyone, with the intention of harming
their honor, their delicacy or the respect due to their authority, contempt
in the exercise of their functions or on the occasion of this exercise, a
magistrate, public officer, commander or agent of the force
public, either by words, gestures, threats, sending or handing over an object
of any kind, either in writing or drawing not made public.
When contempt towards one or more magistrates or assessors -
jurors are appointed at the hearing of a court or tribunal,
imprisonment is one to two years.
In all cases, the trial court may, in addition,
order that its decision will be posted and published under the conditions
that it determines, at the expense of the convicted person, without these costs being able to
exceed the maximum fine provided for above.
Section 264
Is considered outrage and punished as such, done by
person to report to public authorities an offense that they know
not have existed or to produce false proof relating to a
imaginary offense, or to declare before the judicial authority to be
the author of an offense which he neither committed nor contributed to
commit.

- 121 - Article 265
Contempt against constituted bodies is punished in accordance with the
provisions of article 263, paragraphs 1 and 3.
Section 266
The following penalties are imposed in paragraphs 1 and 3 of Article 263:
1° Public acts, words or writings which, as long as a matter is not
not irrevocably judged, are intended to put pressure on the
decisions of magistrates;
2° Public acts, words or writings which tend to bring discredit
on jurisdictional decisions and which are likely to undermine
the authority of justice or its independence.
Section 267
Is punished by imprisonment of three months to two years, anyone
commits violence or assault against a magistrate, a
public official, commander or law enforcement agent in
the exercise of his functions or during this exercise.
When violence results in bloodshed, injury or
illness, or take place either with premeditation or ambush, or against
a magistrate or an assessor-juror at the hearing of a court or a
court, the imprisonment is two to five years.
When violence leads to mutilation, amputation, deprivation
from the use of a limb, blindness, loss of eye or other infirmity
permanent, the penalty incurred is imprisonment for ten to twenty years.
When violence leads to death, without intention of
given, the penalty incurred is imprisonment for twenty to thirty years.
When violence leads to death, with the intention of
give, the penalty incurred is death.
The culprit, sentenced to a prison sentence, may, in
in addition, be subject to a residence ban for a period of two to
five years.

Anyone who is punished with imprisonment of six months to three years

public authority.

destroy evidence or exhibits in criminal proceedings,

Any theft committed with the breaking of seals is punished as theft committed
with break-in under the conditions provided for in article 510.
Section 275
The guard is punished by imprisonment of one to six months, when the
breaking the seals was facilitated by his negligence.

Anyone who knowingly
damages, destroys, misappropriates or removes papers, registers, acts or
effects, kept in archives, registries or public deposits, or handed over to
a public depositary in this capacity.
When the deterioration, destruction, diversion or
the kidnapping was committed, either by the public depositary, or with
violence against people, imprisonment is ten to twenty years.

SECTION I OF THE ASSOCIATION OF CRIMINALS AND
ASSISTANCE FOR CRIMINALS
(Articles 293 to 299)
Section 293
Any association or agreement, regardless of its duration and number
of its members, formed or established for the purpose of preparing or
committing crimes against persons or property constitutes the
crime of criminal association which exists by the sole fact of the
resolution to act taken jointly.
Section 294
Is punishable by imprisonment for five to ten years, any individual who
part of the association or agreement defined in the preceding article.
The imprisonment is ten to twenty years for the leaders of
the association or the agreement or for those who have exercised a
any command.
Section 295
Except in cases of complicity provided for in article 129, is punishable by
imprisonment of five to ten years, anyone, knowingly and voluntarily,
provides members of the association or cartel with weapons,
munitions or instruments of crime, or monetary contributions,
means of subsistence, correspondence or transport, i.e. a
place of meeting, housing or retirement or which helps them to have access to
product of their misdeeds, or which, in any other way, harms them
assistance.
However, the trial court may exempt from the penalty
incurs relatives or allies up to the fourth degree, inclusive,
of one of the members of the association or agreement, when they have only
provided to the latter accommodation or personal means of subsistence.

- 113 - Article 296
Benefits from an absolute excuse, under the conditions provided for in the
articles 143 to 145, that of the culprits who, before any attempted crime
being the subject of the association or agreement and before any prosecution
started, was the first to reveal to the authorities the agreement established or
the existence of the association.
Article 297
Those who, apart from the cases provided for in articles 129, 4°, 196 and 295
have voluntarily concealed a person knowing that they had committed
crime or that she was wanted for this reason by the justice system, or who,
knowingly evaded or attempted to evade arrest
or searches or helped him to hide or flee, are
punishable by imprisonment of one month to two years and a fine of
200109 to 1,000 dirhams
or one of these two penalties only.
Are excepted from the provisions of the preceding paragraph, parents and
allies of the criminal up to the fourth degree inclusive.
Section 298
The persons designated in the preceding article benefit from a
absolute excuse, under the conditions provided for in articles 143 to 145,
when the person concealed or assisted is subsequently recognized
innocent.
Section 299
Except in the case provided for in article 209, is punishable by the imprisonment of a
months to two years and a fine of 200110 to 1,000 dirhams or one
of these two penalties only, anyone who has knowledge of a crime
already attempted or consumed, did not immediately notify the authorities.
Penalties are doubled when the victim of the crime or
The victim of the attempted crime is a child under the age of eighteen.
Are exempt from the provisions of the preceding paragraphs parents and
allies of the criminal up to the fourth degree inclusive, except in what

109 - Ibid.
110 - Ibid.

- 114 - concerns crimes committed or attempted against minors under the age of ten
eight years old111.
SECTION I BIS: FROM PROVOCATION TO CRIMES AND OFFENSES112
Article 299 -1
Except in the cases of participation provided for in article 129 hereof
law and unless more severe penalties are provided for by law, is
punishable by imprisonment of three months to one year and a fine of
5,000 to 50,000 dirhams or one of these two penalties only
anyone who has directly provoked one or more people to
commit a crime or misdemeanor, either by speech, cries or threats uttered
in public places or meetings, or by posters displayed at
public view or by any means meeting the condition of
advertising including electronically, on paper and by
audiovisual, if the provocation was not followed by effect.
However, if the provocation to commit crimes or offenses was
taken effect or resulted in an attempt to commit them, the penalty
incurred will be imprisonment of one year to five years and a fine of
5,000 to 100,000 dirhams or one of these two penalties only.
SECTION II OF THE REBELLION
(Articles 300 to 308)
Article 300
Any attack or resistance practiced with violence or means
in fact towards civil servants or representatives of authority
public acting for the execution of orders or orders emanating from
of this authority, or laws, regulations, judicial decisions, mandates
of justice, constitutes rebellion.
Threats of violence are assimilated to the violence itself.

111 - Article supplemented by article two of law no. 24-03 modifying and supplementing the code
criminal, cited above.
112- Chapter V was supplemented by section I bis, under article 1 of law no.
73-15, cited above.

- 115 - Article 301
Rebellion committed by one or two people is punishable by
imprisonment of one month to one year and a fine of 60 to 100
dirhams113.
If the culprit or one of them was armed, the imprisonment is three
months to two years and a fine of 200114 to 500 dirhams.
Article 302
Rebellion committed in a meeting of more than two people is
punishable by imprisonment of one to three years and a fine of 200115 to
1,000 dirhams.
The penalty is imprisonment of two to five years and a fine of
200116 to 1,000 dirhams if in the meeting more than two individuals were
bearers of visible weapons.
The penalty laid down in the preceding paragraph is individually applicable.
to any person found with a hidden weapon.
Article 303
Are considered weapons for the application of this code,
all firearms, all explosives117, all devices, instruments or objects
piercing, blunt, sharp or suffocating118.

Anyone who provokes it is punished as a co-author of the rebellion,
either by speeches given in public places or meetings, or by

public.

or sentenced by non-irrevocable decision, already detained for another
offense, the sentence pronounced for this rebellion is cumulative, by
exemption from article 120, with any temporary custodial sentence
pronounced for this other offense.

Section 308
Anyone who, by assault, opposes the execution of work

SECTION II BIS VIOLENCE COMMITTED WHEN
THE OCCASION OF COMPETITIONS OR EVENTS

Article 308 -1
Without prejudice to more serious penal provisions, is punishable by
imprisonment of 1 to 5 years and a fine of 1.2 00 to 20,000
dirhams, anyone who participates in acts of violence during or on occasion
competitions or sporting events or their
broadcast in public, during which acts were committed
resulting in death, under the conditions provided for in article 403 of the
this code.
However, the instigators and provocateurs of the facts mentioned in
paragraph above are punishable by the penalties provided for in article 403 hereof.
code.
Article 308 -2
Without prejudice to more serious penal provisions, is punishable by
imprisonment of 3 months to 2 years and a fine of 1,200 to 10,000
