- 118 - dirhams or one of these two penalties only, anyone who participates in
acts of violence during or on the occasion of competitions or
sporting events or their broadcast in public, during
from whom he is struck or inflicted injuries or any other
violence or assault.
However, the instigators and provocateurs of the facts, mentioned in
paragraph above are punishable by the penalties provided for by this code for
punish acts constituting offenses of assault and battery or
any other violence or assault.
Article 308 -3
Without prejudice to more serious penal provisions, is punishable by
imprisonment of 3 months to 1 year and a fine of 1,200 to 10,000
dirhams or one of these two penalties only, anyone who participates in
acts of violence during or at the o
occasion of competitions or
sporting events or their broadcast in public, during
of which there was damage to real property or
movable property of others.
However, the penalty is doubled for the instigators and
provocateurs of the facts mentioned in the preceding paragraph.
Article 308 -4
The provisions of articles 308 -1, 308 -2 and 308 -3 are applicable
acts of violence committed during or on the occasion of competitions or
sporting events or their broadcast on public roads,
public places or in means of public transport,
stations or in any other public place, whether committed before, after or
in conjunction with the progress of the competition, the
demonstration or their retransmission.
Article 308 -5
Without prejudice to the most serious penal provisions, is punishable by
imprisonment of one to 6 months and a fine of 1,200 to 10,000
dirhams or one of these two penalties only, whoever incites
or on the occasion of competitions or sporting events or their
broadcast in public, through speeches, cries, calls, slogans,
banners, images, statues, sculptures or by any other means, at the
racial discrimination or hatred towards one or more
people because of their national or social origin, color, sex,

- 119 - family situation, state of health, disability, political opinion,
union membership, membership or non-membership, true or
supposed, to a specific ethnicity, nation, race or religion.
Anyone who holds by one of the means is punished with the same penalty.
mentioned in the preceding paragraph, defamatory or insulting remarks
meaning of articles 442 and 443 of this code or utters remarks
contrary to morals and public morality with regard to one or more
several people or one or more organizations.
Article 308 -6
Without prejudice to more serious penal provisions, is punishable by
imprisonment of 3 months to 1 year and a fine of 1,200 to 20,000
dirhams or one of these two penalties only, whoever throws
voluntarily during competitions or sporting events, on
one or more people, in the place where the public or the
players, or on the playing field, ring or racetrack,
stones, solid or liquid objects, rubbish, materials
hot objects or any other instrument or object likely to cause harm
to others or to facilities, commits an act of violence likely to
disrupt the progress of a competition or event
sport, or prevents or hinders, by any means, its
unfolding.
Article 308 -7
Without prejudice to more serious penal provisions, is punishable by
imprisonment of 2 to 6 months and a fine of 1,200 to 10,000
dirhams or one of these two penalties only, anyone who deteriorates
or destroyed, by any means, the equipment of stadiums or
sports facilities.
Article 308 -8
Without prejudice to more serious penal provisions, are punished
with a fine of 5,000 to 50,000 dirhams, those responsible for
the organization of sporting activities which do not take appropriate measures
provided for by law, by regulatory texts or by the statutes of
sports organizations to prevent violence during competitions or
sporting events, when this results in acts of violence.
Persons responsible for applying the rules are punished with the same penalty.
measures referred to in the preceding paragraph, when their negligence or

- 122 - failure to apply said measures resulted in acts of
violence.
Article 308 -9
Without prejudice to more serious penal provisions, is punishable by
imprisonment of 1 to 3 months and a fine of 1,200 to 5,000
dirhams or one of these two penalties only, anyone who enters or
attempts to enter a sports venue or a public place where
takes place or is transmitted a competition or a sporting event
by possessing, without legitimate reason, a weapon within the meaning of article 303 of the
this code, laser pointers, burning materials or
flammable or any other instrument or object likely to be used
to commit an act of violence, assault, damage or
destruction of installations or an instrument whose possession is
prohibited by law or by sporting regulations.
Article 308 -10
Without prejudice to more serious criminal provisions, is punishable by
fine of 1,200 to 10,000 dirhams for anyone who enters or attempts to enter
in a state of intoxication or under the influence of narcotic substances or
psychotropic drugs or by possessing alcoholic beverages or
psychotropic drugs, in a sports hall or any other place
public where a competition or a competition takes place or is transmitted
sporting event.
Article 308 -11
Without prejudice to the provisions
more serious criminal offenses, is punishable by
fine of 1,200 to 5,000 dirhams, anyone who enters or attempts to
enter by force or fraud, into a sports venue, soiled
sports or in any other place where a competition or a
sporting event.
Without prejudice to more serious penal provisions, is punishable by
same penalty for anyone who enters or attempts to enter, without legitimate reason,
at the playing field, ring or racetrack, during the course
of a competition or sporting event.
Article 308 -12
Without prejudice to more serious criminal provisions, is punishable by
fine of 1,200 to 10,000 dirhams, anyone who sells

- 121 - tickets for competitions or sporting events, for a fee
price higher or lower than that set by the bodies authorized to set
their price or without their authorization.
Article 308 -13
The fines provided for in articles 308 -1 to 308 -12 above are
increased from double to quintuple, when the author of the offense is a
legal person.
Article 308 -14
In the event of a repeat offense, the penalties imposed against the perpetrators
offenses provided for in articles 308 -1 to 308 -12 are doubled.
Anyone who has been, through a decision, having committed
acquired the force of res judicata, convicted for one of the offenses
provided for in articles 308 -1 to 308 -12 above, has committed the same offense
within five years after the expiration of this sentence or its limitation period.
For the purposes of this provision, are considered to be
constituting the same offense, all the offenses provided for in this section.
Article 308 -15
In the event of conviction for one of the offenses provided for in
articles 308 -1 to 308 -12 above, the court may order the
confiscation for the benefit of the State, subject to the rights of third parties of good
faith, objects and things which were used or were to be used for the offence, or
which are the products thereof, as well as donations or other advantages which have
served or were intended to be used to reward the perpetrator of the offense.
Article 308 -16
The court may, in accordance with the provisions of article 48 of
this code, order that the sentencing decision be published,
broadcast by various audio-visual means or displayed.
Article 308 -17
The court may order the dissolution of the legal entity in
case of his conviction for one of the offenses provided for herein
section.

- 122 - Article 308 -18
In addition to the sanctions provided for in articles 308 -1 to 308 -12 herein
code, the court may order the convicted person prohibited from attending
to competitions and sporting events, for a period
not exceeding two years.It may pronounce the provisional execution of
said measure.
The court may also assign the convicted person a place of
residence or any other place or require him to go to the police stations
police or local authority at the time of competitions or
sporting events which he was prohibited from attending.
Violations of the provisions of the 1st and 2nd paragraphs are punishable by
the penalty provided for in article 318 of this code.
The public prosecutor notifies the decision prohibiting attendance at the
competitions and sporting events to authorities and organizations
provided for in article 308 -19 below in order to ensure its execution.
Article 308 -19
The government authority responsible for sport, federations,
sports clubs, the local commission to combat violence in
sports venues, created by a particular text, the authorities and the force
public and the officers of the judicial police are responsible, each in this
which concerns him, of the execution of judicial decisions pronouncing
the ban on attending competitions and sporting events.
SECTION III ESCAPES
(Articles 309 to 316)
Article 309
Anyone who is,
by virtue of a warrant or a court decision, legally arrested or
detained for crime or misdemeanor, escapes or attempts to escape, or from the premises
assigned to detention by the competent authority, either from the place of work,
or during a transfer.
The culprit is punished with imprisonment of two to five years, if
the escape takes place or is attempted with violence or threats against the
persons, with break-in or breaking of prison.

- 123 - Article 310
The sentence pronounced, in execution of the provisions of article
precedent, against the prisoner who escaped or who attempted to escape, is cumulative,
by way of derogation from article 120, with any temporary custodial sentence of
freedom imposed for the offense which motivated the arrest or
detention.
If the prosecution of this last offense is terminated by a
order or judgment of dismissal or a decision of acquittal or
of absolution, the
of the preventive detention suffered on this count
is not counted against the length of the sentence handed down for escape or
escape attempt.
Article 311
Commanders-in-chief or subordinates, either of the gendarmerie,
either of the armed force or of the police, serving as escort or garrisoning the
posts, prison administration officials and all other
responsible for the custody or conduct of prisoners, are punished, in the event of
of negligence having permitted or facilitated an escape, of a
imprisonment of one month to two years.
Section 312
Is guilty of connivance to escape and punished with imprisonment
from two to five years, any person designated in the preceding article who
procures or facilitates the escape of a prisoner or who attempts to do so,
even without his knowledge, and even if this escape was neither achieved nor
tempted by him;the penalty is incurred even when the aid in the escape has not
consisted only of voluntary abstention.
The penalty can be doubled when the aid consisted of
supply of weapons.
In all cases, the culprit must also be punished with
the ban on exercising any public functions or employment during
ten years at most.
Article 313
Persons other than those designated in article 311 who have
procured or facilitated an escape, or attempted to do so, are punished, even if

- 124 - the escape is not carried out, imprisonment of one to six months and one
fine of 200122 to 500 dirh ams.
If there has been corruption of guards or collusion with them,
the imprisonment is from six months to two years and the fine from 250 to 1,000
dirhams.
When the escape assistance consisted of the provision of a weapon,
the imprisonment is from two to five years and the fine from 250 to 2,000
dirhams.
Article 314
All those who knowingly procured or facilitated an escape
must be jointly ordered to pay damages -
interest owed to the victim or his beneficiaries, in compensation for the damage
caused by the offense for which the escapee was detained.
Article 315
Anyone, for having favored an escape or an attempt
of escape, is sentenced to imprisonment for more than six months, may,
in addition, be subject to the prohibition of one or more of the rights
mentioned in Article 40 and a ban on residence which cannot
exceed five years.
Section 316
Except in the case where harsher penalties are incurred for
conspiracy to escape, is punishable by imprisonment of one to three months
anyone, in violation of a regulation established by the administration
penitentiary or approved by it, delivered or sent or attempted to
deliver or send to a detainee, wherever he is,
sums of money, correspondence or objects of any kind.
Exiting or attempting to exit from
sums of money, correspondence or objects of any kind coming from
of a detainee, carried out in violation of the said regulations.
If the culprit is one of the persons designated in article 311, or if he
is authorized by his functions to freely approach detainees, to

122 - cf.supra note corresponding to article 111.

- 125 - whatever the reason, the penalty is imprisonment of three months to
one year.
SECTION IV NON-OBSERVATION OF FORCED RESIDENCE AND
SAFETY MEASURES
(Articles 317 to 325)
Artic le 317
Anyone who has been sentenced to the criminal penalty of
forced residence defined by article 25, leaves, without the authorization of
the competent authority, the place or the perimeter which had been assigned to it, is
punished by imprisonment of one to five years.
Article 318
If the offense provided for by the preceding article is committed by the person who
been assigned to forced residence as a security measure in application
of article 61, he is punished by imprisonment of six months to two years.
Article 319
Anyone who has been the subject of a residence ban
regularly notified, appears in one of the places which were prohibited to him,
is punishable by imprisonment of six months to two years.
Article 320
Anyone who, in accordance with the provisions of Articles 78, 79,
or 136, is the subject of a decision to be hospitalized in an establishment
psychiatric, evades the execution of this measure, is punished with
imprisonment of three months to one year and a fine of 200123 to 500
dirhams.
Article 321
Anyone who, in accordance with the provisions of article 80, has
the subject of a decision to place in a therapeutic establishment,

123 - Ibid.

- 126 - evades the execution of this measure, is punished by imprisonment
from one to six months and a fine of 200124 to 500 dirhams.
The sentence of imprisonment thus pronounced shall run upon expiration
the investment period;it is combined with the sentence
from em
imprisonment which would have been inflicted by application of article 81.
Section 322
Anyone who, in accordance with the provisions of article 83, has
the subject of a judicial placement decision in an agricultural colony,
evades the execution of this measure, is punishable by imprisonment
from two months to a year.
The prison sentence imposed shall be executed immediately.Its
duration is not counted against that of the placement measure to which the escapee
was submitted.
Section 323
Anyone who, in application of the provisions of article 86, has been
prohibited from exercising, even temporarily, any functions or jobs
public, evades the execution of this measure, is punished with penalties
enacted in article 262.
The same penalties are applicable to anyone who evades
the execution of a measure prohibiting the exercise of a profession, activity
or art, pronounced in execution of article 87.
Article 323 -1125
Is punishable by imprisonment of six months to two years and
fine of 2,000 to 20,000 dirhams or one of these two penalties, any
violation of the prohibitory measure or to contact the victim, to
approach her or communicate with her, by any means
either, or refusal to submit to appropriate psychological treatment
in application of articles 88 -1 and 88 -3 above.
Article 323 -2
Is punishable by imprisonment of one to three months and a fine
from 5,000 to 20,000 dirhams or one of these two penalties only,

Section 324
Any person designated in article 90 - paragraph 2 - who, in violation
the decision to close a commercial or industrial establishment,
contravenes the provisions of the said paragraph, is punishable by imprisonment
from one to six months and a fine of 200 to 2,000 dirhams.
Section 325
Whoever knowingly suppresses, conceals or discards, in its entirety
or in part, posters posted in execution of a judicial decision
taken pursuant to article 48, is punishable by imprisonment of six

SECTION V BEGGAR AND VAGABONDAGE
(Articles 326 to 333)
Article 326
Is punished by imprisonment of one to six months, anyone having
means of subsistence or being able to obtain them through
work or in any other lawful manner, habitually engages in
begging anywhere.
Section 327
Are punished by imprisonment of three months to one year, all
beggars, even disabled or destitute of resources, who request
charity:
1° Either by using threats;
2° Either by simulating wounds or infirmity;
3° Either by being usually accompanied by one or
several young children other than their own descendants;

126 - cf.supra note corresponding to article 111.

- 128 - 4° Either by entering a dwelling or its outbuildings without
authorization of the owner or occupants;
5° Either in a meeting, unless it is the husband and wife, the father and
the mother and their young children, the blind or crippled man and their driver.
Section 328
Those who, either
openly, or under the appearance of a profession, employ
begging of children under thirteen years of age.
Section 329
Is guilty of vagrancy and punished with imprisonment of one to
six months anyone, having neither certain domicile nor means of
subsistence, does not usually practice a trade or profession well
being able to work and who does not justify having requested work or
who refused the paid work offered to him.
Article 330
The father, mother, testamentary guardian, dative guardian, kafil or
the employer and generally any person having authority over a child
or who ensures its protection who delivers, even free of charge, the child,
ward, the abandoned child subject to kafala or the apprentice aged under
of eighteen years to a vagrant or to one or more individuals making
profession of begging, or to several vagabonds is punishable by
imprisonment of six months to two years.
The same penalty is applicable to anyone who delivers or has delivered
the child, the ward, the child subject to kafala or the apprentice, aged
under eighteen years of age, to one or more beggars or to one or more
vagrants, or has determined this minor to leave the home of his
parents, testamentary guardian, tutor
dative, kafil, boss or that of the
person who ensures their protection, to follow one or more
beggars or one or more vagabonds127.

127 - Article supplemented by article two of law n° 24-03 modifying and supplementing the code
criminal, cited above.

- 129 - Article 331
Any beggar, even one, is punishable by imprisonment for one to three years.
invalid, any vagabond, who is found carrying weapons or equipped
instruments or objects capable of committing crimes or offenses.
Section 332
Any vagrant who
carries out or attempts to carry out any act of violence whatsoever against
people, unless due to the nature of this violence a penalty
stronger is incurred by application of another criminal provision.
Section 333
The residence ban may be imposed for a period of five
years against the perpetrators of the offenses provided for in articles 331 and 332 above -
on it.

SECTION I COUNTERFEITING OR FALSIFICATION OF
CURRENCIES OR PUBLIC CREDIT EFFECTS
(Articles 334 to 341)
Article 334
Anyone who counterfeits, falsifies or
alters:
Either metallic currencies, or paper currencies, current
legal in Morocco or abroad;
Either securities, bonds or bonds, issued by the Public Treasury with
its stamp or brand, or interest coupons relating to these securities,
bonds or bonds.

- 132 - Article 335
Are punished with the penalty laid down in the preceding article those who, with
in any way, knowingly participated in the broadcast, in the
distribution, sale or introduction into the territory of the Kingdom
currencies, securities, bonds or bonds designated in said article.
Article 336
Benefits from an absolute excuse under the conditions provided for in the
articles 143 to 145, that of those guilty of the crimes mentioned in both
previous articles which, before the consummation of these crimes and before
all prosecutions, informed the authorities and revealed
the identity of the perpetrators or who, even after the proceedings started, has
procured the arrest of the other culprits.
The individual thus exempted from punishment may nevertheless be prohibited from
stay for a minimum of five years and a maximum of twenty years.
Article 337
Anyone who is punished with imprisonment of six months to three years
colors currencies that are legal tender in Morocco or abroad, in the
purpose of deceiving about the nature of the metal, or emits or introduces into the
territory of the Kingdom of coins thus colored.
The same penalty is incurred by those who participated in the
coloring, issue or introduction of said currencies.
Article 338
He is not punishable who, having received, believing them
authentic, metallic or paper currencies, counterfeit,
falsified, altered or colored, puts them back into circulation in ignorance of
their vice.
The person who puts said currencies back into circulation after having
discovered the defect, is punishable by imprisonment of one to six months and
fine equal to four times the amount thus put back into circulation.
Article 3 39
The manufacture, issue, distribution, sale or introduction
on the territory of the Kingdom of monetary signs intended to
supplement or replace legal tender currencies, is punishable by

- 131 - imprisonment of one to five years and a fine of 500 to 20,000
dirhams.
Section 340
Anyone who manufactures, acquires, holds or transfers products or
material intended for the manufacture, counterfeiting or falsification of
currencies or public credit instruments is punished, if the fact does not constitute
a more serious offense, imprisonment of two to five years and
a fine of 250 to 5,000 dirhams.
Article 341
For the offenses referred to in articles 334 and 338 to 340, the jurisdiction
judgment must necessarily pronounce the confiscation provided for in the
Articles 43, 44 and 89.
SECTION II COUNTERFEITING OF STATE SEALS AND
PUNCHES, STAMPS AND BRANDS
(Articles 342 to 350)
Article 342
Anyone who counterfeits the seal of
the State or uses the counterfeit seal.
The absolutory excuse provided for in article 336 is applicable to the guilty party
of the crime referred to in the paragraph above.
Article 343
Anyone who counterfeits or
falsifies, either one or more national stamps, or one or more
State hammers used for forestry marks, either one or more
hallmarks used to mark gold or silver materials or which make
use of falsified or counterfeit stamps, papers, hammers or punches.
Article 344
Any person who commits
undue
ent procured real stamps, hammers or state hallmarks
designated in the previous article, in fact an application or use
detrimental to the rights and interests of the State.

- 132 - Article 345
Is punished, if the act does not constitute a more serious offense, of
imprisonment of one to six months and a fine of 200128 to 1,000
dirhams or one of these two penalties only, anyone:
1° Manufactures seals, stamps, stamps or marks of the State or
of any authority without the written order of the appointed representatives of
the State or this authority;
2° Manufactures, holds, distributes, buys or sells stamps, seals,
marks or stamps likely to be confused with those of the State or
of any authority, even foreign.
Article 346
Is punishable by imprisonment of one to five years and a fine of
250 to 10,000 dirhams anyone:
1° Counterfeit marks intended to be affixed in the name of the
Government or public service on various species of commodities
or goods or who uses these false brands;
2° Counterfeits the seal, stamp or mark of any authority,
or uses a counterfeit seal, stamp or mark;
3° Counterfeits official letterheads or printed matter in use
in the assemblies established by the constitution, the administrations
public or the different jurisdictions, sells, peddles or distributes them
or makes use of the papers or printed matter thus counterfeited;
4° Counterfeits or falsifies postage stamps, imprints
postage or reply coupons issued by the administration
post office, mobile tax stamps, papers or forms
stamped, sells, peddles, distributes or knowingly uses said stamps,
counterfeit fingerprints, reply coupons, stamped papers or forms or
falsified.
The guilty party may, in addition, be subject to a ban on one or more
several of the rights mentioned in article 40 and a ban on
stay which cannot exceed five years.
Attempting the offenses listed above is punishable
as the offense completed.

128 - cf.supra note corresponding to article 111.

- 133 - Article 347
Is punishable by imprisonment of six months to three years and one
fine of 250 to 5,000 dirhams for anyone who has improperly obtained
real seals, marks or prints provided for in the previous article, in fact
or attempts to make fraudulent application or use of it.
The guilty party may, in addition, be subject to a ban on one or more
several of the rights mentioned in article 40 and a ban on
stay which cannot exceed five years.
Section 348
Is punished by imprisonment of two months to one year and one
fine of 200129 to 1,000 dirhams anyone:
1° Knowingly uses postage stamps, movable stamps or
stamped papers or forms which have already been used or which, by any
means, alters stamps in order to protect them from cancellation and
to thus allow their subsequent reuse;
2° Overload by printing, perforation or any other means
Moroccan postage stamps or other postal fiduciary values, expired
or not, or who sells, peddles, offers, distributes, exports postage stamps
thus overloaded;
3° Counterfeits, imitates or alters stickers, stamps, imprints
postage or reply coupons issued by the postal service
from a foreign country, sells, peddles or distributes said stickers,
stamps, franking impressions or coupons -reply or in fact
knowingly use.
Article 349
Is punishable by imprisonment of one to six months and a fine of
200130 to 2,000 dirhams or one of these two penalties only
anyone:
1° Manufactures, sells, peddles or distributes any objects, printed or
formulas, obtained by any process which, by their form
exterior, present with metal or paper currencies
legal tender in Morocco or abroad, with annuity securities,

129 - Ibid.
130 - Ibid.

- 134 - stickers and stamps of the postal, telegraph and postal service
telephones or state agencies, stamped papers or forms, actions,
bonds, interest shares, dividend coupons or interest relating thereto
and generally with the fiduciary values issued by the State, cities and
public establishments as well as by companies, companies or
private companies, a resemblance likely to facilitate acceptance
said objects, printed matter or formulas in place of values
imitated;
2° Manufactures, sells, peddles, distributes or uses printed matter which,

or any other character, present with letterhead or printed papers
officials in use in the assemblies established by the constitution, the
administered
public ations and the different jurisdictions, a
resemblance likely to cause misunderstanding in the mind of the public.
Section 350
For the offenses defined in this section, the jurisdiction of
judgment must necessarily pronounce the confiscation provided for in
Articles 43, 44 and 89.
SECTION III FORGEMENTS IN PUBLIC WRITING OR
AUTHENTIC
(Articles 351 to 356)
Section 351
Forgery in writing is the fraudulent alteration of the truth, of
nature to cause harm and accomplished in writing by one of the
means determined by law.
Section 352
Any magistrate, any
public official, any notary or adel who, in the exercise of his or her duties
functions, committed a forgery:
either by false signatures;
either by alteration of acts, writings or signatures;
either by supposition or substitution of persons;

- 135 - either by entries made or inserted in registers or on
other public acts, since their preparation or closure.
Section 353
Any magistrate, any
public official, any notary or adel who, by drawing up deeds of
its function, fraudulently distorts the substance or
circumstances, or by writing conventions other than those which have
been traced or dictated by the parties, either by establishing as true
facts that he knew to be false, either by attesting as having been confessed or having
passed in his presence facts which were not, either by omitting or
voluntarily modifying declarations received by him.
Article 354
Any other person is punishable by imprisonment for ten to twenty years.
than those designated in the previous article who commits forgery
authentic and public:
either by forgery or alteration of writing or signature;
either by manufacturing conventions, provisions, obligations or
discharges or by their subsequent insertion in these acts;
either by addition, omission or alteration of clauses, declarations
or facts that these acts were intended to receive and establish;
either by supposition or substitution of persons.
Article 355
Is punishable by imprisonment of one to five years and a fine of
200131 to 500 dirhams any person not party to the act who acts in front
adoul a statement that she knew was not true.
However, benefits from an absolute excuse under the conditions
provided for in sections 143 to 145, the person who, having acted as a witness
in front of adoul a statement not in conformity with the truth, retracted
before harm to others has resulted from the use of the act and
before he himself was the subject of prosecution.

131 - Ibid.

- 136 - Article 356
In the cases referred to in this section, the person who uses the
document which he knew to be false, is punished by imprisonment for five to ten years.
SECTION IV FORGIES IN PRIVATE, COMMERCIAL WRITINGS
OR BANK
(Articles 357 to 359)
Article 357
Any person who in one of the ways provided for in article 354
commits or attempts to commit forgery in commercial or commercial documents
bank is punishable by imprisonment of one to five years and a fine
from 250 to 20,000 dirhams.
The culprit may, in addition, be subject to the prohibition of one or
several of the rights mentioned in article 40 and a ban on
stay which cannot exceed five years.
The penalty may be increased to double the maximum provided for in the first
paragraph when the person guilty of the offense is a banker, a
company director and, in general, a person who has appealed to the
public with a view to the issue of shares, bonds, warrants, shares or securities
of any kind, whether of a company, a commercial enterprise or
industrial.
Section 358
Any person who, in one of the ways provided for in article 354,
commits or attempts to commit forgery in private documents is punishable by
imprisonment of one to five years and a fine of 250 to 2,000
dirhams.
The guilty party may, in addition, be subject to a ban on one or more
several of the rights mentioned in article 40 and a ban on
stay which cannot exceed five years.
Article 359
In the cases referred to in this section, the person who uses the
document that he knew to be false is punishable by the penalties repressing forgery, according to the
distinctions provided for in the two preceding articles.

SECTION VI FALSE TESTIMONY, FALSE OATH AND
THE OMISSION OF TESTIMONY R
(Articles 368 to 379)
Article 368
False testimony is the voluntary alteration of the truth, of a nature
to deceive justice in favor or to the detriment of one of the parties, made
under oath, by a witness during criminal proceedings,
civil or administrative in a deposition that has become irrevocable.
Section 369
Anyone who is guilty of false testimony in matters
criminal, either against the accused or in his favor, is punished by imprisonment
from five to ten years.
If the false witness received money, any reward or
promises, the penalty is that of imprisonment for ten to twenty years.
In the event that the accused is sentenced to a sentence greater than the
confinement in time, the false witness who testified against him incurs this
same sentence.
Article 370
Anyone who is guilty of false testimony in matters
tort, either against the accused or in his favor, is punishable by
imprisonment of two to five years and a fine of 200136 to 1,000
dirhams.
If the false witness received money, any reward or
promises, the prison sentence can be increased to ten years and
the maximum fine is 2,000 dirhams.
Section 371
Anyone who is guilty of false testimony in matters of
simple police, either against the accused or in his favor, is punishable by

136 - Ibid.

- 141 - imprisonment of three months to one year and a fine of 60 to 100
dirhams137.
If the false witness received money, any reward or
promises, the penalty will be imprisonment of six months to
two years and a fine of 200138 to 500 dirhams.
Article 372
Anyone who is guilty of perjury in civil matters
or administrative, is punishable by imprisonment of two to five years and
a fine of 200,139 to 2,000 dirhams.
If the false witness received money, any reward or
promises, the prison sentence can be increased to ten years and
the fine is 4,000 dirhams.
The provisions of this article apply to false testimony
committed in a civil action brought before a criminal court
incidentally to criminal proceedings.
Section 373
Anyone, in any matter, in any stage of a procedure or in
in view of a claim or defense in court, uses promises, offers
or present, pressure, threats, assault, maneuvers or artifices
to induce another to make a deposition or declaration or to
issue a false certificate, is punished, whether the subornation has or
not produced effect, imprisonment of one to three years and a fine
from 200,140 to 2,000 dirhams or one of these two penalties only,
unless the fact constitutes complicity in one of the offenses
serious matters provided for in articles 369, 370 and 372.
Section 374
The interpreter who, in criminal, civil or administrative matters,
knowingly misrepresents the substance of oral statements or documents

(Articles 392 to 448)
SECTION I OF INTENTIONAL HOMICIDE, OF
POISONING AND VIOLENCE
(Articles 392 to 424)
Article 392
Anyone who intentionally causes death to another is guilty
of murder and punished with life imprisonment.
However, murder is punishable by death:
When it preceded, accompanied, or followed another crime;
When its purpose was either to prepare, facilitate or execute a
other crime or misdemeanor, either to encourage flight or to ensure impunity
perpetrators or accomplices of this crime or offense.
Article 393
Murder committed with premeditation or ambush is qualified
assassination and punishable by death.

- 147 - Section 394
Premeditation consists of the design, formed before the action,
to attack the person of a specific individual, or even of one who
will be found or met, even if this design depends on some
circumstance or some condition.
Article 395
Ambushing consists of waiting more or less time, in a
or various places, an individual, either to kill him or to
carry out acts of violence on him.
Article 396
Whoever intentionally kills his father or mother
or any other ascendant is guilty of parricide and punished with the penalty of
dead.
Article 397
Whoever intentionally kills a new child -
born is guilty of infanticide and punished, according to the distinctions provided for in the
articles 392 and 393, the penalties prescribed in these articles.
However, the mother, principal author or accomplice of the murder or
the murder of his newborn child, is punishable by the penalty of
imprisonment of five to ten years, but without this provision being able to
apply to his co-authors or accomplices.
Article 398
Anyone who attempts to take the life of a person through the influence of substances
which can cause death more or less quickly, of some
manner in which these substances were used or administered, and
whatever the consequences, is guilty of poisoning and punished
of death.
Article 399
Anyone who commits an act is punished with the death penalty.
qualified crime employs torture or barbaric acts.

- 148 - Article 400
Anyone who intentionally causes injury or strikes
others or commits any other violence or assault, whether they
did not cause illness or disability, or caused illness
or personal incapacity for work not exceeding twenty days, is
punished by imprisonment of one month to one year and a fine of 200150
to 500 dirhams or one of these two penalties only.
When there has been premeditation or ambush or use of a weapon,
the penalty is imprisonment of six months to two years and a fine of
200151 to 1,000 dirhams.
Section 401
When injuries or blows or other violence or means of violence
fact resulted in incapacity for more than twenty days, the penalty is
imprisonment of one to three years and a fine of 200,152 to 1,000 dirhams.
When there has been premeditation or ambush or use of a weapon,
the penalty is imprisonment of two to five years and a fine of 250 to
2,000 dirhams.
The culprit may, in addition, be punished for at least five years and
ten years at most from the prohibition of one or more of the rights mentioned
in article 40 of this code and the residence ban.
Article 402
When injuries or blows or other violence or means of violence
made have e
nresulted in mutilation, amputation or deprivation of the use of a
limb, blindness, loss of an eye or any other permanent infirmity,
the penalty is imprisonment for five to ten years.
When there has been premeditation or ambush, or use of
weapon, the penalty is imprisonment for ten to twenty years.

The crime of castration is excusable if it was immediately
caused by an indecent assault committed with violence.

- 158 - SECTION II THREATS AND OMISSIONS TO CARRY
RELIEF
(Articles 425 to 431)
Section 425
Anyone, in anonymous or signed writing, image, symbol or
emblem, threat of a crime against persons or property, is
punished by imprisonment of one to three years and a fine of 200160 to
500 dirhams.
Section 426
If the threat provided for in the preceding article was made with an order to
deposit a sum of money in an indicated place or complete any
other condition, the penalty is imprisonment of two to five years and
fines it from 250 to 1,000 dirhams.
Section 427
If the threat provided for in article 425 made with order or under condition
was verbal, the penalty is imprisonment of six months to two years and
the fine of 200161 to 250 dirhams.
Section 428
In the cases provided for in the three preceding articles, the culprits
can, in addition, be imposed for at least five years and ten years at most
the prohibition of one or more of the rights mentioned in article 40 and
of the residence ban.
Section 429
All threats of harm against persons or property, others
than those referred to in articles 425 to 427, by one of the means provided
to the said articles and with order or under condition, are punishable by
imprisonment of one to three months and a fine of 200162 to 250
dirhams or one of these two penalties only.

Anyone who can, without risk for themselves or for third parties,

two sentences only.

- 161 - Article 431 -4
Discrimination sanctions are not applicable to cases
following:
1) discrimination based on health status, when they
consist of operations aimed at prevention and
coverage of risks of death, risks affecting integrity
physical condition of the person or the risk of incapacity to work or
disability;
2) discrimination based on health or disability,
when they consist of a refusal to hire or a justified dismissal
on the medically established incapacity either within the framework of the
labor legislation, or within the framework of the status of the function
public;
3) discrimination based on sex in hiring
when belonging to one or the other sex constitutes, in accordance with the
labor legislation or civil service statutes, the condition
determining the exercise of a job or a professional activity.

only if the incitement to discrimination or hatred between

public or by any means which meets the condition of publicity including

- 162 - SECTION III HOMICIDE AND INVOLUNTARY INJURY
(Articles 432 to 435)
Article 432
Whoever, through clumsiness, imprudence, inattention, negligence or
failure to comply with regulations, involuntarily commits homicide or
is involuntarily the cause is punished by imprisonment of three
months to five years and a fine of 250 to 1,000 dirhams.
Section 433
Whoever, through clumsiness, imprudence, inattention, negligence or
failure to comply with regulations, unintentionally causes injury,
strokes or illnesses leading to further personal incapacity for work
of six days is punishable by imprisonment of one month to two years and
fine of 200168 to 500 dirhams or one of these two penalties
only.
Article 434
The penalties provided for in the two preceding articles are brought to
double when the perpetrator of the offense acted in a state of intoxication, or attempted, either in
fleeing, either by changing the state of the premises, or by any other
means, to escape the criminal or civil liability that he could
incur.
Section 435
Anyone in the cases provided for in articles 607 and 608, 5°, provokes
unintentionally a fire which results in the death of one or more
persons or causes injury to them, is guilty of homicide or
involuntary injuries and punished as such in application of the three articles
previous ones.

SECTION VI TRAFFICKING IN HUMAN BEINGS188
Section 448.1
By human trafficking we mean the act of recruiting a
person, to train them, to transport them, to transfer them, to accommodate them,
to welcome it or to serve as an intermediary for this purpose, through
threat of force, use of force or other forms
coercion, kidnapping, fraud, deception or abuse
authority, function or power or the exploitation of a situation of

187 - Ibid.
188 - The provisions of chapter VII of the first title of book III were supplemented by the
section VI above, under Article 1 of Law No. 27-14 relating to the fight against
trafficking in human beings promulgated by Dahir No. 1 -16-127 of 21 kaada 1437 (August 25
2016);Official Bulletin No. 6526 of 15 Rabii I 1438 (December 15, 2016), p.1952.

- 171 - vulnerability, need or precariousness, or by the fact of giving or
receive sums of money or benefits to obtain the
consent of a person having authority over another person to
operating purposes.
It is not necessary that one of the means provided be used
in the first paragraph above so that we consider that the crime of
Human trafficking is committed against children under the age of
of 18 years, as soon as it turns out that the aim pursued is the exploitation
of said children.
Exploitation includes all forms of sexual exploitation, and
in particular the exploitation of the prostitution of others as well as
exploitation through pornography, including by means
communication and computer communication.Exploitation
also includes exploitation through forced labor, servitude,
begging, slavery or practices similar to slavery,
removal or trafficking of human organs or tissues, exploitation
by means of experiments or medical research carried out on
living beings, or the exploitation of a person for criminal purposes
or in armed conflicts.
Exploitation can only be invoked when it has the effect
to alienate the will of the person and deprive them of the freedom to change
his situation and to undermine his dignity by any means whatsoever.
or even if she received consideration or remuneration for this
effect.
Forced labor within the meaning of this law means any work in
service required of a person under threat and for the execution of which
she did not volunteer.Do not fall under the concept of work
forced the work required for the performance of a military service
compulsory, work required as a result of a conviction
judicial or any work or service required in the event of declaration of the state
emergency.
Section 448.2
Without prejudice to more severe penal provisions, is punishable by
imprisonment of five years to ten years and a fine of 10,000 to
500,000 dirhams anyone who commits the offense of human trafficking
humans.

- 172 - Section 448.3
Without prejudice to more severe penal provisions, the penalty
pronounced for trafficking in human beings is brought to
imprisonment of 10 to 20 years and a fine of 100,000 to
1,000,000 dirhams in the following cases:
1-when the offense
ion is committed under the threat of death,
in fact, torture, kidnapping or defamation;
2-when the perpetrator of the offense was carrying an apparent weapon
or hidden;
3-when the author of the offense is a public fractionalist who
abuses the authority which gives him his position to commit
the offense or facilitate its commission;
4-when the victim suffered from a permanent infirmity, a
incurable organic, psychological or mental illness, due to
the exploitation to which she was subjected under the offense of human trafficking
human beings;
5-when the offense is committed by two or more people
as authors, co-authors or accomplices;
6- when the perpetrator of the offense has become accustomed to committing it;
7-when the offense is committed against several
people in a meeting.
Section 448.4
The offense of trafficking in human beings is punishable by
imprisonment of 20 to 30 years and a fine of 200,000 to
2,000,000 dirhams in the following cases:
1-When the offense was committed against a minor
under eighteen years old;
2-When the offense is committed against a person in
a difficult situation due to age, illness, disability
or a physical or psychological weakness or towards a woman
pregnant whether her pregnancy is apparent or known to her culprit;
3-When the perpetrator of the offense is the spouse of the victim, one
of his ascendants or descendants, his guardian, his kafil, responsible for ensuring
over her or having authority over her.

- 173 - Section 448.5
Without prejudice to more severe penal provisions, the offense of
trafficking in human beings is punishable by imprisonment of 20 to 30 years and
a fine of 1,000,000 to 6,000,000 dirhams, when it is
committed by an organized gang or on a transnational scale, or if the crime
led to the death of the victim.
The penalty provided for in the first paragraph above is increased to imprisonment.
life imprisonment if the offense is committed through torture or acts of
barbarism.
Section 448.6
Is punishable by a fine of 1,000,000 to 10,000,000 dirhams for any
legal person who commits the crime of trafficking in human beings without
prejudice to the sanctions applicable to the natural person who
represents, administers or works on its behalf.
In addition, the court must order the dissolution of the person
morality and the application of the security measures set out in article 62 of the
this law.
Section 448.7
Is punishable by imprisonment of one year to five years and a fine
from 5,000 to 50,000 dirhams, anyone who has become aware that a
person has committed or started to commit a trafficking offense
human beings without reporting it to the competent authorities.
However, the benefit of an exculpatory excuse for the person’s sentence
who refrains from denouncing the author of the offense when that person
is the spouse of the perpetrator of the offense, or one of his ascendants or
descendants.
Section 448.8
Is punishable by imprisonment of one year to five years and a fine
from 5,000 to 50,000 dirhams whoever uses force threatens to do so
resort to or promise to grant an advantage in order to prevent
person to provide testimony or produce evidence,
encourage him to give false testimony, to refrain from presenting
evidence, or to present false statements or evidence relating to
to the offense of trafficking in human beings before any authority
competent and during the various stages of the related trial.

- 174 - Section 448.9
Is punishable by imprisonment of one year to five years and a fine
from 5,000 to 50,000 dirhams anyone who intentionally endangers
the life of a victim of human trafficking or a witness to
deliberately revealing one's identity or place of residence or by
hindering the protective measures taken in its favor.
By victim of human trafficking we mean any person
physical, whether Moroccan or foreign, who suffers harm
proven material or moral result directly from human trafficking
humans, in accordance with the definition given to human trafficking
humans which is provided for by this law.
Section 448.10
Is punishable by imprisonment of one year to five years and a fine
from 5,000 to 50,000 dirhams to anyone, while knowingly knowing that he
is the offense of trafficking in human beings, benefits from a service,
benefit or work from a victim of human trafficking
human beings.
The penalty is doubled if the victim of human trafficking
humans is a minor person under the age of 18.
Section 448.11
Attempt to commit the offenses provided for herein
section is liable to the same penalty provided for the completed crime.
Section 448.12
Get an excuse
absolution of the penalties provided for herein
section that of the culprits who took the initiative to bring to
knowledge of the competent authorities of the information elements of which
it provides with regard to the offense of trafficking in human beings, and
this before any execution or start of execution of this
infringement or by allowing consumption to be prevented.
In the event of denunciation of the offense, the guilty denouncer
may benefit from an excusal of the sentence or its
mitigation, depending on the circumstances of the denunciation, if it allows the
competent authorities, during the investigation, to carry out
the arrest of the other culprits.These provisions do not apply

- 175 - to offenses resulting in death, permanent disability or
incurable organic, psychological or mental illness of the victim.
Section 448.13
Subject to the rights of third parties in good faith, are confiscated
benefit of the Treasury the funds and objects which were used or were to be used to
the commission of the offense of trafficking in human beings, or who are
the proceeds of the commission of this offense.
In addition, the publication of the decision should be ordered
judicial conviction, to display it or to disseminate it by the
audio-visual means.
Section 448.14
The victim of human trafficking is not held responsible
criminally or civilly for any act committed under threat, when
this act is directly linked to the fact that she is personally a victim of
human trafficking, unless they have committed an offense
of her own will without being under threat.

SECTION I ABORTION
(Articles 449 to 458)
Article 449
Whoever, by food, beverages, medicines, maneuvers,
violence or by any other means, procured or attempted to procure
the abortion of a pregnant or presumed pregnant woman, whether
consented or not, is punishable by imprisonment of one to five years and one
fine of 200189 to 500 dirhams.
If death results, the penalty is imprisonment for ten to twenty years.

- 176 - Article 450
If it is established that the offender habitually engaged in the acts
covered by the preceding article, the prison sentence is increased to
double in the case provided for in the first paragraph, and the penalty of imprisonment
extended from twenty to thirty years in the case provided for in paragraph 2.
In the event that under the provisions of article 449 or
present article, only a criminal penalty is incurred, the guilty party may,
in addition, be punished for at least five years and at most ten years
the prohibition of one or more of the rights mentioned in article 40 and of
the ban on residence.

Doctors, surgeons, health officers, dentists, wise men -

in addition, pronounced against the guilty, either temporarily or as
definitive.

Is punishable by imprisonment of six months to two years and one
fine of 200191 to 500 dirhams the woman who intentionally
has had an abortion or has attempted to do so or who has consented to the use of

- 179 - SECTION II EXPOSURE AND REDUCTION OF
CHILDREN OR THE INCAPABLED
(Articles 459 to 46 7)
Article 459
Whoever exposes or abandons in a solitary place, a child of
less than fifteen years old or someone incapable, unable to protect themselves
even because of his physical or mental state, is, for this fact alone,
punished by imprisonment of one to three years195.
If exposure or neglect resulted from illness or
incapacity for more than twenty days, the penalty is imprisonment for two
at five years old.
If the child or incapable person remains mutilated or crippled, or if he is
remained suffering from a permanent disability, the penalty is imprisonment for five
at ten years old.
If exposure or neglect caused death, the penalty is
imprisonment for ten to twenty years.
Article 460
If the culprits are the ascendants or any other persons
having authority over the child or incapable person, or having custody, the penalty:
Is imprisonment of two to five years in the cases provided for in 1st
paragraph of the preceding article;
-Is increased to double that decreed by paragraph 2 of this article
in the case provided for in said paragraph;
Is imprisonment for ten to twenty years in the case provided for in the 3rd paragraph
of said article;
Is imprisonment for twenty to thirty years in the case provided for in the 4th paragraph
of said article.

Anyone who exposes or abandons in a non-solitary place, a child

from two to five years.

judgment of conviction, the penalty is imprisonment for five to ten years.

Article 483
Whoever, by his voluntary state of nudity or by the obscenity of
his gestures or his actions, commits a public outrage against modesty is punished
imprisonment of one month to two years and a fine of 200217 to
500 dirhams.
Contempt is considered public as soon as the fact which constitutes it
was committed in the presence of one or more unwitting witnesses or
minors aged eighteen, or in a place accessible to the view of the
public.

modesty consumed or attempted without violence, on the person of a minor
under the age of eighteen, an incapacitated person, a handicapped person or a

the other sex218.

consumed or attempted with violence against persons of one or more
the other sex.

under eighteen years of age, of an incapacitated person, of a handicapped person, or on a
person known for weak mental abilities, the culprit is
punished with imprisonment for ten to twenty years219.

Article 497
Anyone who excites, promotes or facilitates debauchery or prostitution
minors under eighteen years of age, is punishable by imprisonment of

dirhams226.

- 196 - Article 4 98
Is punishable by imprisonment of one year to five years and a fine
from five thousand to one million dirhams, unless the fact constitutes
a more serious offense, anyone who knowingly:
1) in any way helps, assists, or protects the
prostitution of others or solicitation with a view to prostitution;
2) in any form, knowingly, perceives
a share of the proceeds of prostitution or debauchery of others or
receives subsidies from a person habitually engaged in
prostitution or debauchery;
3) lives, knowingly, with a person engaging in
usually to prostitution;
4) hires, trains, delivers, protects, even with consent
or exerts pressure on a person with a view to prostitution or
debauchery or with a view to continuing to practice prostitution or
debauchery;
5) acts as an intermediary, in any capacity, between the
persons engaging in prostitution or debauchery and individuals
who exploit or pay for the prostitution or debauchery of others;
6) helps the person who exploits the prostitution or debauchery of others to
provide false justifications for their financial resources;
7) finds himself unable to justify the source of his income,
considering his standard of living while he lives with a person engaging in
usually engaged in prostitution or debauchery or maintaining
suspicious relationships with one or more people engaged in
prostitution or debauchery;
8) hinders actions of prevention, control, assistance or
rehabilitation undertaken by sectors, bodies or organizations
authorized for this purpose with regard to people who engage in
prostitution or debauchery or who are exposed to them227.

the penal code, cited above.

The penalties decreed in the preceding article are brought to
imprisonment of two to ten years and a fine of ten thousand to two
million dirhams when:
1) the offense was committed against a minor under the age of ten -
eight years old;
2) the offense was committed against a person in a
difficult situation due to age, illness, disability or
a physical or psychological weakness, or with regard to a pregnant woman,
that her pregnancy is apparent or known by the culprit;
3) the offense was committed against several people;
4) the perpetrator is one of the spouses or belongs to
one of the
categories listed in article 487 of this code;
5) the offense was provoked by duress, abuse of authority, or
fraud, or when means which allow photographing,
film or record were used.
6) the offense is committed by a person charged, by reason of his
function, to participate in the fight against prostitution or debauchery228, to
the protection of health and youth or the maintenance of order
public;
7) the perpetrator of the offense was carrying an apparent weapon or
hidden;
8) the offense was committed by several people as
authors, co-authors or accomplices without constituting a gang;
9) the offense was committed through messages addressed to
through the means of communication either to an undetermined public or
to specific people229.

sexual237.

2. by written, telephone or electronic messages,

sexual.

Anyone who provokes, incites or facilitates the exploitation of children

by any means, a real, simulated or perceived sexual act or

sexual activity, is punishable by imprisonment of one year to five years and

The same penalty is applicable to anyone who produces, distributes, publishes,
imports, exports, exhibits, sells or possesses pornographic materials
similar.
These acts are punished even if their elements are committed outside
of the Kingdom.
The penalty provided for in the first paragraph of this article is brought to
double when the author is one of the child's ascendants, a person
responsible for his protection or having authority over him.
The same penalty is applicable to attempts to commit these acts.
The judgment of conviction orders the confiscation and
destruction of pornographic materials.
The court may order the publication or display of the judgment.
In addition, the judgment may order, where appropriate, the withdrawal of the
license of which the convicted person is the beneficiary.He can also pronounce
temporary or permanent closure of premises239.

SECTION I THEFT AND EXTORTION
(Articles 505 to 539)
Article 505
Anyone who fraudulently removes anything belonging to
another is guilty of theft and punished with imprisonment of one to five years
and a fine of 200,241 to 500 dirhams.
Article 506
By way of derogation from the provisions of the preceding article, is qualified
ie
larceny and punishable by imprisonment of one month to two years and one
fine of 200242 to 250 dirhams for fraudulent subtraction of a thing
of low value belonging to others.

241 - cf.supra note corresponding to article 111.
242 - Ibid.

- 223 - Thefts committed with the aggravating circumstances provided for in
Articles 507 to 510 constitute theft punishable by the penalties prescribed
to said articles.
Section 507
Individuals guilty of
theft, if the thieves or one of them were obviously carrying or
concealed weapon within the meaning of article 303, even if the theft was committed
by a single person and in the absence of any other circumstances
aggravating.
The same penalty is applicable if the culprits or one of them
had the weapon in the motor vehicle that took them to the scene
of the offense or which they would have used to ensure their escape.
Section 508
Individuals are punished with imprisonment of twenty to thirty years.
guilty of theft committed on public roads or in vehicles
used for the transport of passengers, connections or
baggage, or within the confines of railways, stations, ports, airports,
landing or boarding platforms, when the theft was committed
with at least one of the circumstances referred to in the following article.
Section 509
Individuals are punished with imprisonment of ten to twenty years.
guilty of theft committed with at least two circumstances
following:
If the theft was committed with violence, or threats of violence, or
illegal wearing of a uniform, or usurpation of a position of authority;
If the theft was committed at night;
If the theft was committed in a meeting by two or more people;
If the theft was committed using climbing, external break-in or
interior, underground opening, false keys, or broken seals,
in a house, apartment, room or dwelling, inhabited or used
to the home or their outbuildings;
If the perpetrators of the theft have secured the disposal of a vehicle
motorized in order to facilitate their enterprise or encourage their escape;

- 224 - If the perpetrator is a servant or hired servant, even when he has
committed theft from people he did not serve, but who
found either in his employer's house or in the house where he
accompanied him;
If the thief is a worker or apprentice, in the house, workshop or
store of his employer or if he is an individual working
usually in the home where he stole.
Section 510
Guilty individuals are punished with imprisonment of five to ten years.
of theft committed with only one of the following circumstances:
If the theft was committed with violence, or threats of violence, or
illegal wearing of a uniform, or usurpation of a position of authority;
If the theft was committed at night;
If the theft was committed in a meeting, by two or more people;
If the theft was committed using climbing, external break-in or
interior, underground opening, false keys or broken seals,
even in a building not used for habitation;
If the theft was committed during a fire or after a
explosion, collapse, flood, shipwreck, revolt,
a riot or other disturbance;
If the theft concerned an object which ensured the security of a means of
transport of any kind, public or private.
Article 511
Any building, accommodation, lodge, tent, is deemed to be an inhabited house.
even mobile cabin, which, even without being currently inhabited, is
intended for housing and everything that depends on it such as courses, low -
courtyards, barns, stables, buildings enclosed therein, whatever they may be
usage and even if they would have a particular fence in the
fence or general enclosure.
Article 512
A break-in is defined as forcing or attempting to force a
any closure system either by breaking or damaging it, or
in any other way to allow a person to enter

- 225 - in a closed place, or to seize something contained in a
closed place or in a closed cabinet or container.
Article 513
Climbing is qualified as any entry into houses, buildings,
courtyards, lower courtyards, buildings of any kind, gardens, parks and enclosures,
carried out over walls, doors, roofs or any other fence.
Article 514
Fake keys, all hooks, imitated, counterfeit or
altered or which were not intended by the owner or tenant for
whatever closures the culprit used.
Is also considered a false key, the real key
unduly withheld by the culprit.
Article 515
Anyone who counterfeits or alters keys is punished with
imprisonment of three months to two years and a fine of 200243 to
500 dirhams.
If the culprit is a professional locksmith, imprisonment is
from two to five years and a fine of 250 to 500 dirhams unless the fact
does not constitute an act of complicity in a more serious offense.
Section 516
Public roads are considered to be roads, tracks, trails
or any other places dedicated to public use, located outside
urban areas and where any individual can freely move around at any time
day or night, without legal opposition from anyone.

- 227 - Item 517244
Whoever steals horses or beasts from the fields,
car or mount, large and small livestock, or instruments
agricultural is punishable by imprisonment of one to five years and a fine
from 50,255 to 5,005 dirhams.
The same penalties apply to the theft of wood from fellings,
stones in the quarries, sand in the beaches, in the dunes
coastal areas, in valleys or in its natural places, as well as the theft of
fish in pond, fishpond or reservoir.
However, when it comes to the crime of theft of sand in the places
provided for in the preceding paragraph, the stolen quantity of which has been determined,
the fine is 500 dirhams per cubic meter without it being able to be
less than 1,200 dirhams.Any fraction of a cubic meter is considered
as cubic meter.
The court also orders confiscation for the benefit of the State,
subject to the rights of third parties in good faith, machines, objects,
things and means of transport which were used or were to be used to
the offense or which are the proceeds thereof, as well as donations or other
advantages which served or were intended to serve to reward the author of
the offense.

Anyone who steals from the fields of crops or other production
useful of the earth, already detached from the ground, even put in sheaves or in

a fine of 200,245 to 250 dirhams.
If the theft was committed, either at night, or by several people, or
using vehicles or carrying animals, the imprisonment is one
to five years and fines from 200246 to 500 dirhams.

- 213 - SECTION II OF SCAM AND ISSUING CHECKS
WITHOUT PROVISION
(Articles 540 to 546)
Section 540
Anyone, with a view to obtaining or providing to a third party, a
illegitimate pecuniary profit, cleverly misleads a
person by false assertions, or by the concealment of
true facts, or cleverly exploits the error where there was a
person and thus induces them to acts harmful to their interests
pecuniary or those of a third party, is guilty of fraud and punished with
imprisonment of one to five years and a fine of 500 to 5,000
dirhams.
The prison sentence is doubled and the maximum of
the fine of 100,000 dirhams if the culprit is a person who has committed
call to the public for the issue of shares, bonds, bonds, shares
or any securities, either of a company or of an enterprise
commercial or industrial.
Section 541
Immunities and restrictions on the exercise of public action
enacted by articles 534 to 536 are applicable to the offense of fraud
provided for in the first paragraph of article 540.
Section 542
Is punishable by the penalties for fraud provided for in the first paragraph of
article 540, anyone in bad faith:
1° Has inalienable property;
2° In fraud of the rights of a first contracting party, gives goods
"in rahn" or usufruct, in pledge or rental or dispose of it in a way
any;
3° Continues the recovery of a debt already extinguished by payment
or innovation.

- 214 - Article 543
Is punished by the penalties laid down in the first paragraph of article 540, without
that the fine may be less than the amount of the check or
insufficiency, anyone in bad faith:
1° A, either issued a check without prior and available funds or
with a provision lower than the amount of the check, is withdrawn, after
the issue, all or part of the provision, is a defense to the drawee of
pay;
2° Agreed to receive a check issued under the conditions provided
in the previous paragraph261.

that the amen of may be less than the amount of the check, whoever
issues or accepts a check on the condition that it is not cashed
immediately but kept as a guarantee222 bis.

SECTION III ABUSE OF TRUST AND OTHERS
ILLEG ITIMES APPROPRIATIONS
(Articles 547 to 555)
Section 547
Anyone in bad faith misappropriates or dissipates to the detriment of
owners, possessors or holders, either of effects, money or
goods, i.e. tickets, receipts, writings of any kind containing
or operating obligations or discharges and which had been given to him at the
condition of returning them or making a specific use or use of them,
is guilty of breach of trust and punished with imprisonment of six
months to three years and a fine of 200,262 to 2,000 dirhams.
If the damage suffered is of low value, the duration of the sentence
imprisonment will be from one month to two years and the fine from 200263 to 250
dirhams subject to the application of the causes of aggravation provided for
in articles 549 and 550.

- 216 - Article 548
Immunities and restrictions on the exercise of public action
enacted by articles 534 to 536 are applicable to the offense of abuse of
trust provided for in article 547.
Article 549
If the breach of trust is committed:
Either by an adel, receiver, curator, judicial administrator
acting in the exercise or in the course of their duties;
Either by an administrator, employee or guardian of a foundation
pious, to the detriment of this foundation;
Either by an employee or employee to the detriment of his employer or
offender, the penalty is imprisonment of one to five years and a fine
from 200,264 to 5,000 dirhams.
Section 550
The penalty of imprisonment decreed in article 547 is brought to
double and the maximum fine is 100,000 dirhams if the abuse of
trust was committed by a person appealing to the public in order to
to obtain, either on his own account or as director,
director or agent of a company or commercial enterprise
or industrial, the remittance of funds or values as a deposit, mandate
or collateral.
Article 551
Anyone who has received advances for execution
of a contract, refuses without legitimate reason to execute this contract or to
repay these advances, is punishable by imprisonment of one to six months and
a fine of 200,265 to 250 dirhams.
Article 552
Anyone who abuses needs, passions or inexperience
a minor aged twenty-one or any other incapable or prohibited person,
to make him subscribe to his prejudice, obligations, discharges or

264 - Ibid.
265 - Ibid.

- 217 - other acts involving his assets, is punishable by imprisonment of
six months to three years and a fine of 200,266 to 2,000 dirhams.
The prison sentence is one to five years and the fine is 250 to
3,000 dirhams if the victim was placed under the custody, surveillance or
the authority of the culprit.
Article 553
Whoever, abusing a blank document entrusted to him, has
fraudulently written above an obligation or release, or any
other act which may compromise the person or assets of the
signatory, is punishable by imprisonment of one to five years and
fine of 200,267 to 5,000 dirhams.
In the event that the blank signature had not been entrusted to him, the culprit
is prosecuted as a forger and punished with the penalties laid down in articles
357 or 358, according to the distinctions provided for in the said articles.
Section 554
Anyone after having produced in a dispute
administrative or judicial, any document, title or memory, subtracts it

commerce, cited above, taking into account those contained in article 733 of the said law.
Article 721: In the event of the opening of a treatment procedure, are guilty of bankruptcy
the persons mentioned in article 702 against whom one of the following facts has been reported:
1) intend to avoid or delay the initiation of the processing procedure, or
makes purchases with a view to resale below the price, or uses ruinous means
to raise funds;
2) having misappropriated or concealed all or part of the debtor's assets;
3) having fraudulently increased the debtor's liabilities;
4) having kept fictitious accounts or caused accounting documents to disappear
the company or company or having abstained from keeping any accounts when the law requires it
the obligation.
Article 722: Bankruptcy is punishable by one year to five years of imprisonment and a fine.
from 10,000 to 100,000 dirhams or one of these two penalties only.
Accomplices in bankruptcy incur the same penalties, even if they do not have the status of
business leaders.
The penalty provided for in the first paragraph is doubled when the bankrupt is a manager,
de jure or de facto, of a company whose shares are listed on the stock exchange.
Article 723: Persons guilty of the offenses provided for in this section are liable to
also, as an accessory penalty, the commercial forfeiture provided for in Chapter II of the
this title.
Article 725: For the application of the provisions of sections 1 and 2 of this chapter, the
prescription of public action only runs from the day of the judgment pronouncing the opening of
the processing procedure when the facts in question appeared before that date.
Article 726: The criminal court is seized either of the prosecution of the public prosecutor, or
upon constitution of civil party of the trustee.
The provisions provided for in article 710 are applicable.
Article 727: The public prosecutor may request from the trustee the delivery of all documents and
documents held by him.
See also articles 62 to 68 of the commercial code which include other sanctions
relating to certain commercial acts.
See also the criminal offenses and sanctions provided for in Law No. 17-95 relating to
limited companies, promulgated by Dahir No. 1 -96-124 of 14 Rabii II 1417 (August 30, 1996),
Official Bulletin No. 4422 of 4 Jumada II 1 417 (October 17, 1996), p.661, and articles 100 and
