- 219 - Is guilty of bankruptcy and punished with the penalties decreed at the
this section depending on whether this banking route is simple or
fraudulent, any merchant in a state of cessation of payments who, either
negligently or intentionally committed culpable acts
likely to harm its creditors.
Section 557
Is guilty of simple bankruptcy and without imprisonment
from three months to three years, any trader in a state of cessation of
payment which has:
1° Either through his lifestyle, through games or bets, engaged in
expenses deemed excessive;
2° Is spent large sums, in pure operations
chance or in fictitious stock market or commodity transactions;
3° Either, with the intention of delaying the recognition of the cessation of
its payments, makes purchases with a view to reselling it below the price
or, with the same intention, used ruinous means to obtain
funds;
4° Be paid, after cessation of his payments, a creditor to the
harm to others;
5° Has already been declared bankrupt twice when these two bankruptcies
were closed due to insufficient assets;
6° Fails to keep accounts;
7° Is practicing his profession contrary to a prohibition provided for
by law.
Section 558
Is guilty of simple bankruptcy and punished with the penalty provided for in
the preceding article, any merchant in a state of cessation of payment who,
in bad faith, has:
1° Is contracted on behalf of others, without receiving values
in exchange, commitments considered too considerable given its
situation when he contracted them;
2° Either failed to meet the obligations of a previous arrangement
and been declared bankrupt;

- 222 - 3° Either failed to file with the registry, within fifteen days of the cessation
of its payments, the declaration of this cessation and the filing of its
balance sheet;
4° Either fails to be near
enter in person with the trustee, in the cases and
within the set deadlines;
5° Either presented incomplete or irregular accounting
outfit.
Article 559
In the event of cessation of payment by a company, penalties are imposed
of simple bankruptcy, the administrators, directors or liquidators
of a limited company, the managers or liquidators of a company
limited liability and in general, all agents
social, who have in this capacity and in bad faith:
1° Large sums belonging to the company are spent in
making operations of pure chance or fictitious operations;
2° Either, with the intention of delaying the recognition of the cessation of
payments from the company, makes purchases with a view to resale below
of the course or, with the same intention, employed ruinous means of
procure funds;
3° Either, after cessation of payments from the company, paid or made
pay one creditor to the detriment of others;
4° Is made to contract by the company, on behalf of others, without
that it receives values in exchange, commitments deemed too
considerable having regard to her situation when she contracted them;
5° Is kept or causes the company's accounts to be kept irregularly.
Article 560
Are punished with the penalties of simple bankruptcy,
administrators, directors or liquidators of a limited company, the
managers or liquidators of a limited liability company and a
generally speaking, all corporate officers who, in order to subtract
all or part of their assets to the prosecution of the company in a state of
cessation of payment or those of partners or corporate creditors
have, in bad faith, misappropriated or concealed all or part of their property,
or who have fraudulently recognized themselves as debtors of sums that they do not
should not.

- 221 - Article 561
Is guilty of fraudulent bankruptcy and punished with
imprisonment of two to five years, any trader in a state of
cessation of payment which has subtracted its accounts, misappropriated or
dissipated all or part of its assets or which, either in its writings or by
public acts or commitments under private signatures, either in
his balance sheet, fraudulently recognized himself debtor of sums that he did not
shouldn't have.
The culprit may, in addition, be punished for at least five years and
ten years at most from the prohibition of one or more of the rights mentioned
in article 40 of this code.
Article 562
In the event of cessation of payment by a company, penalties are imposed
of fraudulent bankruptcy the directors, directors or
liquidators of a limited company, the managers or liquidators of a
limited liability company and in general, all
corporate officers who, fraudulently, withdrew the books from the
company, misappropriated or concealed all or part of its assets or which, either
in the writings, either by public acts or commitments under
private signatures, either in the balance sheet, recognized the debtor company of
are that she shouldn't.
Article 563
The following are punished with the penalties of fraudulent bankruptcy:
1° Persons convinced of having, in the interest of the debtor,
subtracted, concealed or concealed all or part of his movable property or
buildings, unless the fact constitutes one of the acts of complicity
provided for in section 129;
2° Persons convicted of having fraudulently produced
fictitious claims in bankruptcy, either in their name or through the interposition of
people;
3° Persons who, trading under the name of another or
under an assumed name, are guilty of one of the acts provided for
in article 561;
4° Persons practicing the profession of stockbroker or
stock broker found guilty of even simple bankruptcy.

- 222 - Article 564
The spouse, descendants or ascendants of the debtor or their
relatives or allies up to the fourth degree inclusive who, without having
acted in complicity with him, embezzled, entertained or concealed property
furniture likely to be included in the bankruptcy estate, are punished
imprisonment of six months to three years and a fine of 200,270 to
3,000 dirhams.
Article 565
The creditor who has stipulated, either with the debtor, or with all
other persons, special advantages because of their vote in the
deliberations of the mass, is punishable by the penalties provided for in article
previous.
Article 566
Any bankruptcy trustee who is guilty of embezzlement in his
management is punishable by the penalties provided for in article 549.
Article 567
Accomplices to simple or fraudulent bankruptcy are punished
the same sentences as the main perpetrator, even if they do not have the quality
of trader.
Article 568
In all cases provided for in this section, the guilty party may, in
in addition, be subject to the ban on practicing the profession, decreed by
the arti
key 87.
Article 569
All judgments and judgments of conviction rendered under the
this section, are, at the expense of the convicted person, displayed and published in a
newspaper authorized to receive legal announcements.

SECTION V INFRINGEMENTS ON REAL ESTATE PROPERTY
(Article 570)
Article 570
Is punishable by imprisonment of one to six months and a fine of
200271 to 500 dirhams, anyone who by surprise or fraud dispossesses another
of real estate property.
If the dispossession took place either at night, or with threats or
violence, either with the help of escalation or ef fraction, or by several
persons, either with visible or hidden weapons carried by one or
several of the perpetrators, the imprisonment is from three months to two years and
the fine of 200272 to 750 dirhams.
SECTION VI CONCEALMENT OF THINGS
(Articles 571 to 574)
Article 571
Anyone who knowingly conceals things in whole or in part,
subtracted, diverted or obtained with the help of a crime or an offense, is
punished by imprisonment of one to five years and a fine of 200,273 to
2,000 dirhams, unless the act is punishable by a penalty
criminal as constituting an act of complicity in a crime provided for by
section 129.
However, the receiver is punished with the penalty prescribed by law for
the offense with the help of which things were subtracted, diverted
or obtained in all cases where this penalty is less than the penalty
provided for in the preceding paragraph.
Article 572
In the event that the penalty applicable to the perpetrators of the offense using
from which things have been subtracted, diverted or obtained, is a

271 - Ibid.
272 - Ibid.
273 - Ibid.

- 224 - criminal penalty, receivers incur the same penalty if they are
convinced of having had, at the time of the concealment, knowledge of the circumstances
to which the law attaches this criminal penalty.
However, the death penalty is replaced with regard to the receiver by
that of perpetual reclusion.
Article 573
In the event of a criminal conviction, the person guilty of concealment
may, in addition, be punished for at least five years and at most ten years
the prohibition of one or more of the rights mentioned in article 40 of the
this code.
Section 574
Immunities and restrictions on the exercise of public action
enacted by articles 534 to 536 are applicable to the offense of concealment provided for
in articles 571 and 572.

condemned.

SECTION VII OF SOME ATTACKS TO PROPERTY

intentionally or negligently and for profit, exposes its author to penalties
provided for in the penal code.The amount of the fine is set by the court taking into account the
gains that the defendant derived from the violation.
Judicial authorities have the authority to increase the upper limit of penalties to three times
when the offender is convicted of a new act constituting a violation of rights
less than five years after being convicted of a prior violation.
The authorities
judicial s also apply the measures and sanctions referred to in articles 59 and
60 of the Code of Criminal Procedure, provided that a decision concerning these sanctions has not been
not yet taken into a civil suit.
Measures, reparations and sanctions in the event of abuse of technical means and alteration of
information on the rights regime.

prevent or restrict the reproduction of a work or to deteriorate the quality of the
copies or copies made;

Article 575
Anyone who publishes writings, compositions on Moroccan territory
musical, drawings, paintings or any other production, printed or

from 200281 to 10,000 dirhams, whether these works were published in Morocco
or abroad.

the export and import of counterfeit works.

Is guilty of counterfeiting and punished by the penalties provided for in article
precedent, anyone who reproduces, represents or distributes, by any

b) The manufacture or importation, for sale or rental, of a device or means of

receive it;
c) The deletion or modification, without being authorized to do so, of any information relating to the
rights regime in electronic form;
(d) Distribution or importation for the purpose of distribution, broadcasting,
communication to the public or making available to the public, without being authorized to do so, of works
of performances, phonograms or broadcasts knowing
that rights management information in electronic form has
been deleted or modified without authorization.
(e) For the purposes of this Article, “rights management information” means
information enabling the author, work, performing artist to be identified,
the interpretation or performance, the producer of phonograms, the phonogram, the organization
broadcasting, the broadcast broadcast, and any right holder under this law,
or any information relating to the conditions and terms of use of the work and others

or modified, are assimilated to copies or infringing copies of works.

- 232 - SECTION VIII DESTRUCTIONS, DEGRADATION AND
DAMAGE
(Articles 580 to 607)
Article 580
Anyone who intentionally sets fire to buildings, dwellings,
lodges, tents, even mobile cabins, ships, boats, stores,
construction sites, when they are inhabited or used for habitation and
generally in places inhabited or used for habitation, whether they
belong or do not belong to the perpetrator of the crime, is punishable by
dead.
Anyone who voluntarily sets a fire is punished with the same penalty,
either to vehicles, aircraft or wagons containing people, or to
wagons not containing people but forming part of a
convoy which contains them.
Article 581
Whoever, when these goods do not belong to him, puts
intentionally set fire:
Either to buildings, accommodation, lodges, tents, even cabins
mobiles, ships, boats, stores, construction sites, when they are neither
inhabited, nor used for habitation;
Either to vehicles or aircraft not containing people;
Either to forests, woods, copses or to wood arranged in piles or cubic meters;
Either to standing crops, to straw or to crops in piles or
in millstones;
Either to wagons, loaded or not with goods or other objects
furniture not part of a convoy containing people, is
punished with imprisonment for ten to twenty years.
Article 582
Whoever sets fire or causes any property to be set on fire
listed in the preceding article and belonging to it, voluntarily causes
any harm to others, is punishable by imprisonment of five to ten
years.

- 231 - The same penalty is incurred by anyone who sets a fire on the orders of the
owner.
Section 583
Anyone who intentionally sets fire to objects
whatever, belonging to him or not, and placed in such a way as to
communicate the fire, set fire by this communication to one of the
property belonging to others listed in article 581, is punishable by
imprisonment of five to ten years.
Article 584
In all the cases provided for in articles 581 to 583, if the fire
deliberately provoked resulted in the death of one or more
persons, the person guilty of the fire is punished by death.
If the fire caused injury or disability
permanent es, the penalty is that of reclusion perpetua.
Article 585
The penalties set out in articles 580 to 584 are applicable,
according to the distinctions provided for in the said articles, to those who destroy
voluntarily, in whole or in part, or attempt to destroy, by the effect
a mine or any other explosive substances, buildings,
accommodation, lodges, tents, cabins, ships, boats, vehicles of all
kinds, wagons, aircraft, stores or yards or their dependencies and,
generally, all movable or immovable objects of any nature
whatever.
Article 586
Anyone who intentionally destroys or attempts to destroy, by the effect
a mine or any other explosive substances, routes
public or private, dikes, dams or roads, bridges,
port or industrial installations, is punishable by imprisonment of twenty
at thirty years old.
Section 587
Anyone who voluntarily places an explosive device on a track
public or private, is punishable by imprisonment for twenty to thirty years.

- 232 - Article 588
If the offenses provided for in articles 586 or 587 resulted from the
death of one or more people, the culprit is punished with death;if
the offense caused injury or permanent disability, the
penalty is that of perpetual reclusiveness.
Section 589
Benefits from an absolute excuse under the conditions provided for in the
articles 143 and 145 that of those guilty of one of the offenses listed
to articles 585 to 587 which, before the completion of this crime and before
all prosecutions, gave notice and revealed the identity
ity of
authors to the administrative or judicial authorities or who, even after
the proceedings begun, brought about the arrest of the other culprits;
he may however be subject to a stay ban measure for
a duration of ten to twenty years.
Article 590
Whoever intentionally destroys or overthrows, by any means
whether in whole or in part, buildings, bridges, dykes,
dams, roadways, port or industrial installations that he knew
belong to someone else or which causes the explosion of a steam engine,
either the destruction of a motor forming part of an installation
industrial is punishable by imprisonment for five to ten years.
If it resulted from the offense provided for in the preceding paragraph a
homicide, injury or permanent disability to a third party, the
guilty is punished by death if there has been homicide and by imprisonment of ten to
twenty years in all other cases.
Article 591
Anyone, with a view to causing an accident or hindering or
obstruct traffic, place an object on a road or public path
obstructing the passage of vehicles or uses a means
any means to obstruct their progress, is punishable by imprisonment.
from five to ten years.
If the offense provided for in the preceding paragraph resulted in
homicide, injury or permanent disability to a third party, the
guilty is punished by death if there has been homicide and by imprisonment of ten to
twenty years in all other cases.

- 233 - Article 592
Except in the cases provided for in article 276, anyone who voluntarily burns
or destroyed in any way, registers, minutes or acts
originals of the public authority, securities, notes, bills of exchange,
commercial or bank instruments, containing or operating an obligation,
disposal or discharge, is punishable by imprisonment for five to ten years if the
destroyed parts are acts of public authority, effects of
commerce or banking, and imprisonment of two to five years and
a fine of 200282 to 500 dirhams if it concerns any other document.
Article 593
Incurs the penalties set out in the preceding article, following the
distinctions provided for in said article, unless the fact constitutes a
more serious offense, anyone who knowingly destroys, removes, conceals,
conceals or alters a public or private document likely to facilitate the
investigation of crimes or offenses, discovery of evidence or punishment
of their author.
Article 594
Perpetrators of looting or devastation of foodstuffs, goods or
other movable property, committed in a meeting or gang and by open force,
are punished by imprisonment for ten to twenty years, unless the act
constitutes a more serious offense, such as one of the crimes provided for in
articles 201 and 203.
However, those who prove to have been trained by
provocations or solicitations to take part in these disorders, will be
punished with imprisonment for five to ten years.
Article 595
Anyone who intentionally destroys, slaughters, mutilates or degrades:
Either monuments, statues, paintings or other objects intended for
utility or public decoration and raised or placed by authority
public or with its authorization;
Either monuments, statues, paintings or objects of art of any kind
placed in museums, places reserved for worship or other open buildings

fine of 200,283 to 500 dirhams.

any instruments used in manufacturing, is punishable by
imprisonment of one month to two years and a fine of 200,284 to
1,000 dirhams.
If the offender is a factory worker or employee of

places, buildings, enclosures and outbuildings or on land whose master
of the killed or mutilated animal is the owner, tenant or farmer, is punished
imprisonment of two to six months and a fine of 200292 to 250
dirhams.

Article 603
Whoever, without necessity, kills or mutilates one of the animals
mentioned in article 601, is punished:
If the offense was committed in the places where the offender is
owner, tenant or farmer, imprisonment of six days to

two sentences only;
If the offense was committed in another place,
imprisonment of fifteen days to three months and a fine of 200294
at 300 dirhams.
Section 604
In the cases provided for by articles 597 to 602, if the act was committed
either during the night, or in hatred of a public official and because of
his functions, the culprit is punished with the maximum penalty provided for by
the article punishing the offense.
Section 605
In the cases provided for by articles 596, 597 and 601, the guilty party may,
in addition, be punished for at least five years and at most ten years
the prohibition of one or more of the rights mentioned in article 40 of the
this code and the ban on residence.
Article 606
Whoever, in whole or in part, fills ditches, destroys
fences, of whatever materials they are made, cut or torn
live or dry hedges, move or remove bollards or all
other marks planted or recognized to establish the boundaries between
different properties, is punishable by imprisonment of one month to one year
and a fine of 200,295 to 500 dirhams.

- 237 - Anyone who voluntarily diverts public waters without right
or private is punishable by imprisonment of one month to two years and
fine of 200,296 to 5,000 dirhams.
Section 607
Anyone, except in the cases provided for in articles 435 and 608, 5°, determines
by clumsiness, carelessness, inattention or non-observance of
regulations, fire of movable or immovable properties
of others, is punishable by imprisonment of one month to two years or
fine of 200,297 to 500 dirhams.
SECTION IX DIVERSIONS OF AIRCRAFT,
DAMAGE TO AIRCRAFT AND DAMAGE OF
AIR NAVIGATION FACILITIES298
Article 607a
Anyone on board an aircraft in flight seizes this
aircraft or exercises control over it, by violence or by any other means,
is punishable by imprisonment for ten to twenty years.
Anyone who voluntarily commits threats or violence to
against flight personnel on board an aircraft in flight,
with a view to diverting it or compromising its security, is punishable by
imprisonment of five to ten years, without prejudice to the more serious sanctions that
could incur by application of articles 392 and 403 of the penal code.
For the application of the two preceding articles299, an aircraft is
considered to be in flight from the moment when
boarding being
finished, all its exterior doors were closed, until the
moment when one of these doors is opened in preparation for disembarkation.
In the event of a forced landing, the flight is expected to continue until
that the competent authority takes charge of the aircraft as well as the
people and property on board.

296 - Ibid.
297 - Ibid.
298 - Section added by article 2 of the dahir carrying law n° 1 -74-232 of 28 rabii II 1394 (21
May 1974) cited above.
276 - The legislator rather aimed at “the two preceding paragraphs….".

- 238 - Without prejudice to the application of the provisions of articles 580, 581
and 585 of the penal code, anyone who voluntarily harms an aircraft in
service for damages which render it unfit for flight or which are of a
to compromise his safety in flight, is punishable by imprisonment of five to ten
years.
An aircraft is considered to have been in service since
where the ground staff or crew begin to prepare it for a
determined flight until the expiration of a period of twenty-four hours
following any landing.The period of service extends in any state of
cause to the entire time during which the aircraft is in flight at
meaning of paragraph III above.
Article 607b
Anyone who destroys or
damages air navigation installations or services or
disrupts operation if one of these acts is likely to
compromise the safety of the aircraft, or communicate information
which he knows to be false, with the aim of compromising this security.

Article 607 -3
The fact of fraudulently accessing all or part of a
automated data processing system is punished by one to three months
months of imprisonment and a fine of 2,000 to 10,000 dirhams or

Any person who remains in

300 - Chapter added by the single article of law no. 07 -03 supplementing the penal code with regard to
concerns offenses relating to automated data processing systems,

Article 607 -4
Without prejudice to more severe penal provisions, is punishable by six
months to two years of imprisonment and from 10,000 to 100,000 dirhams
fine anyone who commits the acts provided for in the preceding article against
all or part of an automated data processing system
believed to contain information relating to internal security or
external state or secrets concerning the national economy.
Without prejudice to more severe penal provisions, the penalty is

fine dirhams when it results from acts punished in the first paragraph nea
of this article or the modification or deletion of data
contained in the automated data processing system, or
an alteration of the functioning of this system or when said acts
are committed by a civil servant or an employee during the exercise of his duties
functions or on the occasion of this exercise or if it facilitates
achievement to others.
Article 607 -5
Intentionally obstructing or distorting the
operation of an automated data processing system and
punished by one year to three years of imprisonment and from 10,000 to 200,000
dirham fine or one of these two penalties only.
Article 607 -6
Fraudulently entering data into a system
automated data processing or damage or delete
or fraudulently modify the data it contains, their method of
treatment or transmission, is punishable by one year to three years
imprisonment and a fine of 10,000 to 200,000 dirhams or one
of these two sentences only.
Article 607 -7
Without prejudice to more severe penal provisions, forgery or
falsification of computerized documents, whatever their form, of
likely to cause harm to others, is punishable by imprisonment
from one year to five years and a fine of 10,000 to 1,000,000 dirhams.

- 242 - Without prejudice to dis
more severe penal positions, the same punishment
is applicable to anyone who knowingly uses the documents
computerized systems referred to in the preceding paragraph.
Article 607 -8
Attempting the offenses provided for in articles 607 -3 to 607 -7 above
and by article 607 -10 below is punishable by the same penalties as the offense itself -
same.
Article 607 -9
Anyone who has participated in a formed association or agreement
established for the purpose of preparation, evidenced by one or more facts
material, one or more offenses provided for in this chapter
is punishable by the penalties provided for the offense itself or for
the most severely punished offense.
Article 607 -10
Is punishable by imprisonment of two to five years and a fine
from 50,000 to 2,000,000 dirhams makes it, for any person,
make, acquire, hold, transfer, offer or make available
arrangement of equipment, instruments, computer programs
or any data, designed or specially adapted to commit the
offenses provided for in this chapter.
Article 607 -11
Subject to the rights of the third party in good faith, the court may
pronounce the confiscation of the materials used to commit the
offenses provided for in this chapter and the thing which is the
product.
The culprit may, in addition, be punished for a period of two to
ten years of the ban on the exercise of one or more of the rights
mentioned in article 40 of this code.
The inability to perform any public function or employment for a
duration of two to ten years as well as the publication or display of the
sentencing decision may also be made.

SECTION I OF 1ST CLASS OFFENSES
(Article 608)

Section 608
Are punished by detention of one to fifteen days and a fine of
20 to 200 dirhams or one of these two penalties only302:
1° Perpetrators of assault or minor violence;
2° Those who voluntarily throw hard bodies,
garbage or any other materials likely to contaminate the
clothing;
3° Those who, through clumsiness, imprudence, inattention, negligence or
failure to comply with regulations, unintentionally cause injury,
strokes or illnesses leading to equal personal incapacity for work
or less than six days;
4° Those who exhibit or cause to be exhibited on the public highway, or in
public places with posters or images contrary to decency.The
judgment of condemnation will order the removal of the object(s)
incriminated, which, if it is not voluntary, will be, notwithstanding all
remedies, carried out ex officio and without delay at the expense of the convicted person;
5° Those who cause fire to movable property or
other people's real estate:
Either by obsolescence or lack of repairs or cleaning of
furnaces, chimneys, forges, houses and factories located nearby;

SECTION II 2ND CLASS OFFENSES
(Article 609)
Article 609
The following are punished with a fine of 10 to 120 dirhams303:
Contraventions relating to public authority
1° Those who, being able to do so, refuse or negate
intelligent to do the work, the
service or to provide the assistance for which they have been legally required, within the
circumstances of accidents, tumults, shipwrecks, floods, fires or
other calamities, as well as in cases of banditry, looting, blatant
crime, public outcry or judicial execution;
2° Those who, legally required, refuse to give their name and
address or give inaccurate names and addresses;

303 - 1st paragraph of article 609 of the penal code amended by law no. 3 -80 modifying certain
provisions of the penal code, cited above.

- 243 - 3° Those who, regularly summoned by the authority, abstain
without valid reason to appear;
4° Those who, except in the case provided for in article 341 of the code of procedure
criminal, disrupt the exercise of justice, at the hearing or in any other
location304;
5° Those who refuse entry to their home to an agent of
the authority acting in execution of the law and complying with the
requirements of the code of criminal procedure relating to searches or
home visits;
6° Innkeepers, hoteliers, landlords or renters of furnished houses,
who neglect to register upon arrival, without any blank on a register
regularly kept the surname, first names, position, usual address and date
entry, any person sleeping or spending all or part of the night
in their house as well as when they leave the date of their release;those
of them who, at the times determined by the regulations or when they
are required to fail to represent this register to the qualified authority;
7° Those who, apart from the cases provided for in article 339, accept, hold
or establish means of payment intended to supplement or
to replace legal tender monetary signs;
8° Those who refuse to receive cash and national currencies,
not false or altered, according to the value for which they are valid;
9° Those who use weights and measures different from those
prescribed by current legislation;
10° Those who, without regular authorization, establish or maintain
in the streets, paths, squares or public places of games, lotteries or
other games of chance;
11° Those who contravene decrees and orders legally taken
by the administrative authority when the offenses against these texts are not
not repressed by special provisions.
Violations relating to order and public safety
12° Those who entrust a weapon to an inexperienced person or
not enjoying his mental faculties;
13° Those who allow a madman entrusted to their care to wander;

of any kind or beasts of burden, which contravene the regulations

Contraventions relating to roads and public hygiene
27° Those who degrade or deteriorate, in any way

of use;

domestic animals that they own or care for
has been entrusted to them or who treat them badly by placing an excessive burden on them.
Property violations

SECTION III PROVISIONS COMMON TO THE MISCELLANEOUS
CONTRACTS
(Articles 610 to 612)
Section 610
The following are confiscated under the conditions provided for in articles 44 and 89:

- 248 - Means of payment intended to supplement or
replace the legal tender monetary signs referred to in article 609,
paragraph 7;
The weights and measures referred to in Article 609, paragraph 9;
Tables, instruments, gaming or lottery machines, as well as
stakes, funds, foodstuffs, objects or prizes offered to players, referred to in
article 609, paragraph 10;
Objects purchased or pledged under the conditions provided for in
article 609, paragraph 24, if their legitimate owner has not been
discovered;
The keys and hooks referred to in article 609, paragraph 25;
Instruments, devices or costumes used or intended for
the exercise of the profession of diviner or sorcerer referred to in article 609,
paragraph 35.
Section 611
The offender who, in the twelve months preceding the
contravention, had been the subject of a previous conviction which became
irrevocable for an identical offense, is in a state of recidivism
by application of article 159 and must be punished as follows:
In the event of a repeat offense of one of the contraventions provided for in article 608, the
detention and the fine may be doubled;
In the event of a repeat offense of one of the offenses provided for in article 609, the
fine can be increased to 200 dirhams;detention for six
days, at most, can even be pronounced305.
Section 612
In matters of contravention, the granting of mitigating circumstances
and their effects are determined by the provisions of article 151.
